🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 同样的检索结果，换一句 prompt 答案就不同。质量责任更多压在检索还是 prompt？你怎么分工调优、分别用什么指标？Same retrieved context, different prompt, different answer. Does quality rest more on retrieval or the prompt? How do you split the tuning, and with what metrics each?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：检索决定“依据对不对”、prompt 决定“依据用得对不对”——先把召回调达标，再用 prompt 调忠实度/格式。召回不到，prompt 再好也是巧妇难为无米之炊；指标上，检索看命中率/MRR，prompt 看 Faithfulness 与格式/约束达成率。别把两类问题混在一起调。🔑 Key: retrieval decides whether the evidence is right, the prompt decides whether it's used right — get recall to target first, then tune faithfulness/format with the prompt. No recall, no prompt can save it; measure retrieval by hit-rate/MRR and the prompt by Faithfulness plus format/constraint adherence. Don't conflate the two while tuning.
Prompt A（宽松）Prompt A (loose)
“根据资料回答” → 资料没提保修期，却补一句“一般为一年”(编造)。'answer from the context' → the warranty isn't there, yet it adds 'usually one year' (invented).
vs
Prompt B（严格）Prompt B (strict)
“只用资料、未提及就说不知道” → 老实回答“资料未提及”。'use only the context, say unknown otherwise' → honestly says 'not in the sources'.
检索一字不变，换 prompt 就改变忠实度——这是“最后一公里”Same retrieval, a different prompt changes faithfulness — the 'last mile'
🎯 2. 有人到处用全局 Settings、有人坚持显式传参。各自利弊？你怎么定团队规范？Some use the global Settings everywhere; others pass config explicitly. Trade-offs, and what team convention would you set?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：全局少样板但隐式依赖、难追踪、测试易串味；显式可读可测、可多配置共存但啰嗦。规范：全局设默认值，关键/差异化组件(评估用的 judge、特殊 query engine)显式覆盖并就近声明——既省样板又可追踪。🔑 Key: global means less boilerplate but an implicit, hard-to-trace dependency that can leak state in tests; explicit is readable/testable and lets configs coexist but is verbose. Convention: set sane global defaults, and explicitly override key/divergent components (an eval judge, a special query engine) declared close to use — boilerplate saved, traceability kept.
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 同样的检索结果，换一句 prompt 就能改变答案——这把“质量责任”更多压在检索上还是 prompt 上？你怎么分工调优？Same retrieval, different prompt, different answer — does that put more of the quality burden on retrieval or on the prompt, and how would you split your tuning effort?
第四部分 · 进阶

18 · 进阶检索

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

基础 top-k 不够用时，进阶检索登场：融合多查询（QueryFusionRetriever）、自动合并相邻块（AutoMergingRetriever）、递归（RecursiveRetriever）、按问题路由到不同库（RouterRetriever）。它们都实现同一个 BaseRetriever 接口。When plain top-k isn't enough, advanced retrieval steps in: fuse multiple queries (QueryFusionRetriever), merge adjacent chunks (AutoMergingRetriever), recurse (RecursiveRetriever), and route by question (RouterRetriever). All implement the same BaseRetriever interface.

一个问题One question
→
改写成多版Rephrase to N
LLM 生成 n-1 个LLM writes n-1 more
→
各自检索Retrieve each
每版取 top-ktop-k per variant
→
倒数排名融合Reciprocal rerank
跨多个排名累加summed across rankings
→
合并结果Merged set
去重后的统一列表one deduped list
Query Fusion：一题多问、分别检索，再用 reciprocal rerank 融合成一份结果Query Fusion: ask one question many ways, retrieve each, then reciprocal-rerank into a single result set
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
不只问一次、不只取一处：多角度改写再合并、把碎片拼回完整段落、按问题选对资料库。
Don't ask once or look in one place: rephrase from several angles and merge, stitch fragments back into a passage, and pick the right corpus per question.

基础 top-k 的三类短板，进阶检索逐一补齐Top-k's three weak spots — advanced retrieval patches each

把这些进阶检索当成一堆零散“高级技巧”去记，很容易迷失。换个视角：它们都在补朴素 top-k 相似度检索的三类典型短板——召回不全（换个问法本能命中的内容被漏掉）、命中碎片（块切得太碎，单个 Node 只剩半句上下文）、多库分流（不同问题其实该查不同索引）。看清这三道缺口，下面四种检索器就各有归属——其中“命中碎片”有横向合并、纵向递归两种补法；而且它们都实现同一个 BaseRetriever，可即插即换、互相嵌套。
Memorizing advanced retrieval as a pile of scattered “tricks” gets you lost. Flip the view: they all patch plain top-k's three classic weak spots — missed recall (a different phrasing would have hit, but it's dropped), fragmented hits (chunks so small a single Node holds half a thought), and multiple corpora (different questions belong to different indexes). Name those three gaps and the four retrievers below each find their place — “fragmented hits” gets two cures, merging sideways and recursing down — and since all implement one BaseRetriever, you swap or nest them freely.
基础 top-k 的短板Top-k's weak spot
进阶检索器Advanced retriever
怎么补How it patches
召回不全Missed recall
QueryFusionRetrieverQueryFusionRetriever
一题多版改写再融合，覆盖更多说法multi-rephrase then fuse to cover more phrasings
命中碎片Fragmented hits
AutoMergingRetrieverAutoMergingRetriever
相邻子块自动合并回父块merge adjacent child chunks back into the parent
命中碎片Fragmented hits
RecursiveRetrieverRecursiveRetriever
从摘要/索引节点递归到完整原文recurse from summary/index nodes to the full source
多库分流Multiple corpora
RouterRetrieverRouterRetriever
由 LLM 选择该查哪个索引/工具an LLM picks which index/tool to query
三类短板组织起四种检索器：“命中碎片”有合并与递归两解，其余各对一招——接口统一，可单用也可叠加Three weak spots organize four retrievers: “fragmented hits” has two cures (merge, recurse), the rest map one-to-one — one interface, used alone or stacked
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
retrievers/fusion_retriever.py · QueryFusionRetriever — 多查询融合（含 reciprocal rerank）multi-query fusion (with reciprocal rerank)
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
retrievers/auto_merging_retriever.py · AutoMergingRetriever — 相邻块自动合并auto-merging adjacent chunks
深入：融合检索与可插拔接口Deep dive: fusion retrieval and the pluggable interface点击展开expand
🧪 示例：一题改写成 4 版🧪 Example: rephrase one question into 4
QueryFusionRetriever(retrievers=[base], num_queries=4)：原问题加上 LLM 生成的 3 个改写各自检索，再用 reciprocal rerank 融合成一份去重结果，召回通常明显高于单版 top-k。
QueryFusionRetriever(retrievers=[base], num_queries=4): the original question plus 3 LLM-generated rewrites each retrieve, then reciprocal rerank fuses them into one deduped result set — recall usually beats single-query top-k by a clear margin.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
所有检索器都实现同一个 BaseRetriever，统一返回 list[NodeWithScore]，于是它们能互相嵌套、随意替换，并直接塞进任何 QueryEngine——上层完全无感。
Every retriever implements the same BaseRetriever and returns list[NodeWithScore], so they nest and swap freely and drop straight into any QueryEngine — the layer above never notices.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
num_queries=n 让 LLM 额外生成 n-1 个改写（原问题也算一版）；融合方式由 FUSION_MODES 决定，默认 simple，常显式设 reciprocal_rerank（RRF）——按每条结果在多个排名中的倒数位次累加打分，再统一排序。
num_queries=n makes the LLM generate n-1 extra rewrites (the original counts as one); fusion is governed by FUSION_MODES (default simple), and you commonly set reciprocal_rerank (RRF) — it sums each result's reciprocal rank across the several rankings, then sorts once.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
不是每个问题都靠“多问几遍”：碎片化严重就用 AutoMergingRetriever 合并回父块；知识有层级或引用就用 RecursiveRetriever 跟随引用到原文；面对多个索引就用 RouterRetriever 让 LLM 选库。它们可单用，也能叠在 fusion 之上。
Not every problem yields to “asking more times”: for heavy fragmentation use AutoMergingRetriever to merge back into parents; for hierarchical or cited knowledge use RecursiveRetriever to follow references to the source; for multiple indexes use RouterRetriever to let an LLM pick the corpus. Each works alone or stacked atop fusion.
进阶检索器仍是 BaseRetriever，可直接塞进 QueryEnginestill a BaseRetriever — drops into any QueryEngine
from llama_index.core.retrievers import QueryFusionRetriever

# 把一个问题改写成多版、分别检索，再用 reciprocal rerank 融合
fusion = QueryFusionRetriever(
    retrievers=[index.as_retriever(similarity_top_k=5)],
    num_queries=4,
    mode='reciprocal_rerank',
)
nodes = fusion.retrieve('退款和换货政策有何不同？')
print(len(nodes))
另一种思路：AutoMerging 把命中的碎片拼回完整父块A different angle: AutoMerging stitches hit fragments back into a whole parent
from llama_index.core.retrievers import AutoMergingRetriever
from llama_index.core.node_parser import HierarchicalNodeParser

# 层级切块：同一段文本切成大/中/小三层父子块
parser = HierarchicalNodeParser.from_defaults()
nodes = parser.get_nodes_from_documents(docs)
# ...把叶子块建进 index，得到一个基础 base_retriever...
retriever = AutoMergingRetriever(
    base_retriever,                  # 任意 BaseRetriever（这里检索叶子块）
    storage_context=storage_context,
)
# 命中同一父块的多个叶子，会被自动合并成更完整的父块
merged = retriever.retrieve('保修条款有哪些例外情况？')
print(len(merged))
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 进阶检索针对“召回不全/碎片化/多库”等基础 top-k 的短板。Advanced retrieval targets top-k's weak spots: missed recall, fragmentation, multiple corpora.
  • 它们都实现 BaseRetriever，可无缝接入现有 QueryEngine。All implement BaseRetriever, so they drop into an existing QueryEngine.
  • Fusion 用改写+融合提升召回；AutoMerging 用关系合并提升上下文完整度。Fusion lifts recall via rephrase+merge; AutoMerging lifts context completeness via relationships.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
进阶检索没有免费的午餐：fusion 多跑几轮检索来提召回，但更慢更贵；auto-merging 合并父块补上下文，却可能引入冗余。每一种都是在用更多计算换更好结果。
Advanced retrieval is no free lunch: fusion runs extra retrieval passes to lift recall but costs more and runs slower; auto-merging merges parent blocks to restore context but can add redundancy. Each trades more compute for better results.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. 为什么进阶检索器能直接替换基础检索器、塞进原来的 QueryEngine？Why can advanced retrievers drop into an existing QueryEngine in place of the basic one?
  1. 因为它们更快Because they're faster
  2. 因为它们都实现同一个 BaseRetriever 接口Because they all implement the same BaseRetriever interface
  3. 因为它们是 core 内置的Because they're built into core
  4. 因为它们不用 embeddingBecause they skip embeddings
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：BAnswer: B 统一的 BaseRetriever 接口让检索策略可插拔，QueryEngine 不感知具体实现。The uniform BaseRetriever interface makes retrieval strategies pluggable; the QueryEngine doesn't care which one.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 基础 top-k 召回不全。三类典型短板分别用哪种进阶检索器补？对延迟敏感的线上问答你会上 query fusion 吗？怎么权衡、怎么验证召回真提升？Naive top-k under-recalls. Which advanced retriever fixes each of the three typical weaknesses? Would you use query fusion in latency-sensitive live Q&A? How do you weigh it and verify recall actually improves?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：召回不全→Query Fusion、命中碎片→AutoMerging/Recursive、多库分流→Router；进阶检索是“用更多计算换更好结果”，没有免费午餐。延迟敏感时先量化：fusion 多跑几轮检索+一次改写，提升值不值这点延迟？高价值可容忍几百 ms 才上，否则用更便宜手段(更好 embedding/轻量 rerank/缓存)。验证：对 gold 集比较加 fusion 前后的命中率与端到端质量，再核延迟预算。🔑 Key: under-recall → Query Fusion, fragmented hits → AutoMerging/Recursive, multi-source → Router; advanced retrieval trades more compute for better results — no free lunch. Under latency pressure, quantify first: fusion adds retrieval passes + a rewrite — is the lift worth the latency? Adopt only for high-value, few-hundred-ms-tolerant flows; else use cheaper levers (better embedding/light rerank/caching). Verify by comparing hit-rate and end-to-end quality with/without fusion on a gold set, then re-check the latency budget.

🎯 2. AutoMerging 检索和“直接调大 chunk_size”有何不同？什么时候用 Router？How is AutoMerging retrieval different from 'just use a bigger chunk_size', and when do you use a Router?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：AutoMerging 用小块检索(精准)，命中同一父块的多个小块时再合并成父块喂 LLM(补上下文)——兼得精准与上下文。直接调大 chunk_size 则全程用大块，检索更糊、噪声更多。Router 用于多个 Index/数据源分流：用 selector 把问题路由到最合适的那个。🔑 Key: AutoMerging retrieves with small chunks (precise), then merges small chunks under the same parent into the parent for the LLM (context) — precision and context together. A bigger chunk_size uses large chunks throughout, blurring retrieval and adding noise. A Router is for routing across multiple indices/sources: a selector sends each question to the best one.
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 进阶检索都用更多计算换更好结果。对一个延迟敏感的线上问答，你会接受 query fusion 的额外开销吗？如何权衡？Advanced retrieval trades more compute for better results. For a latency-sensitive live Q&A, would you accept query-fusion's overhead — and how would you weigh it?
第四部分 · 进阶

19 · 评估 Evaluation

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

RAG 到底好不好，不能只凭“感觉还行”。评估器（Evaluator）把答案质量量化成分数，让“好”与“坏”有据可比——下面这张表把核心的几把尺子摆在一起。Is the RAG any good? “Feels fine” isn't an answer. Evaluators quantify answer quality into scores so “good” and “bad” become comparable — the grid below lays out the core rulers.

评估器Evaluator
衡量什么Measures
需要的输入Needs
FaithfulnessEvaluatorFaithfulnessEvaluator
答案是否被检索上下文支撑（防幻觉）is the answer grounded in retrieved context (anti-hallucination)
答案 + source_nodesanswer + source_nodes
RelevancyEvaluatorRelevancyEvaluator
检索与答案是否切合该问题are the context and answer on-topic for the query
问题 + 答案 + source_nodesquery + answer + source_nodes
CorrectnessEvaluatorCorrectnessEvaluator
对照参考答案是否正确（1–5 分）is the answer correct vs a reference (scored 1–5)
问题 + 答案 + 参考答案query + answer + reference answer
三把尺子量不同侧面：忠实看“有没有据”，相关看“切不切题”，正确看“对不对”Three rulers, three facets: faithfulness checks grounding, relevancy checks on-topic, correctness checks rightness
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
评估器就像给作文判卷的老师：不是一句“感觉不错”，而是拿固定的几把尺子逐项打分——分数能横向比较、也能复算。
An evaluator is like a teacher grading essays: not a vague “seems good” but scoring against a fixed set of rulers — numbers you can compare across runs and recompute.

把调优变成可度量的闭环Turn tuning into a measurable loop

没有评估，调 RAG 就是“凭感觉”：改了切块、换了检索、调了 Prompt，到底变好还是变坏，全靠主观印象。评估把它变成一个闭环：每次改动后，用同一套问题和指标跑一遍，对比分数再决定保留还是回退。于是每一步优化都有据可依，也能挡住“修好一个、悄悄弄坏一批”的回归。下面用一组真实感的分数，看这个闭环跑起来是什么样。
Without evaluation, tuning RAG is “by feel”: after changing chunking, retrieval or the prompt, whether it improved is a subjective impression. Evaluation turns it into a closed loop: after each change, run the same questions and metrics, compare the scores, then decide to keep or revert. Every optimization becomes evidence-based, and you catch the “fix one, silently break a batch” regressions. The numbers below show one turn of that loop in action.
基线Baseline
Faithfulness 0.82Faithfulness 0.82
→
改一处Change one
chunk_size 512 → 1024chunk_size 512 → 1024
→
重测Re-measure
同一批问题same question set
→
对比Compare
0.82 → 0.71，↓ 变差0.82 → 0.71, worse ↓
→
决定Decide
回退，守住基线revert, keep the baseline
一次真实的闭环：基线 0.82 → 把 chunk_size 改大反降到 0.71 → 回退；倘若改成加一道 rerank 升到 0.91，就予以保留——分数让去留有据，再回到第一步One real turn of the loop: baseline 0.82 → enlarging chunk_size drops it to 0.71 → revert; had a rerank lifted it to 0.91 you'd keep it — the score makes the call, then back to step one
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
evaluation/faithfulness.py · FaithfulnessEvaluator — 忠实度评估（防幻觉）faithfulness (anti-hallucination)
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
evaluation/base.py · BaseEvaluator.evaluate_response — 统一评估入口the unified evaluation entry
深入：评估器怎么打分Deep dive: how evaluators score点击展开expand
🧪 示例：评一个回答🧪 Example: grade one answer
FaithfulnessEvaluator().evaluate_response(response=resp) 直接吃 QueryEngine 的返回（已含 source_nodes）；结果里 passing 表示是否“有据可依”，score 给出分值。
FaithfulnessEvaluator().evaluate_response(response=resp) consumes the QueryEngine response directly (it already carries source_nodes); the result's passing says whether it is “grounded”, and score gives the value.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
把质量量化，调优才能回归测试：同一套问题在每次改动后复跑，分数升降一目了然，避免“改好一个、悄悄弄坏一批”。
Quantifying quality makes tuning regression-testable: rerun the same question set after each change and the score moves are obvious, so you don't “fix one and silently break a batch”.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
多数评估器是 LLM-as-judge：把问题、答案、上下文（或参考答案）塞进一个评判 Prompt，让 LLM 给判断。Faithfulness / Relevancy 多为二值（passing 是/否），Correctness 则给 1–5 分的 score。
Most evaluators are LLM-as-judge: the question, answer and context (or reference) go into a judging prompt and an LLM rules on it. Faithfulness / Relevancy are usually binary (passing yes/no), while Correctness returns a 1–5 score.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
人工评估最准但慢且贵，适合做小规模“金标准”；LLM 评估快且可自动化，适合每次改动的回归。实践中两者结合：维护一个固定的回归问题集，平时用 LLM 评，定期抽样人评来校准。
Human evaluation is most accurate but slow and costly — good for a small “gold standard”; LLM evaluation is fast and automatable — good for per-change regressions. In practice combine both: keep a fixed regression question set, judge with an LLM routinely, and sample human checks periodically to calibrate.
把“感觉还行”变成“可度量”turn “feels fine” into “measurable”
from llama_index.core.evaluation import FaithfulnessEvaluator

resp = index.as_query_engine().query('退款政策是什么？')
ev = FaithfulnessEvaluator()
result = ev.evaluate_response(response=resp)
print(result.passing, result.score)   # 答案是否有据可依
用 BatchEvalRunner 跑一小批问题，得到可对比的基线Run a small batch with BatchEvalRunner for a comparable baseline
from llama_index.core.evaluation import (
    FaithfulnessEvaluator, RelevancyEvaluator, BatchEvalRunner)

# 用一小批问题跑回归：每题同时算忠实度与相关性
runner = BatchEvalRunner(
    {'faith': FaithfulnessEvaluator(), 'rel': RelevancyEvaluator()},
    workers=4,
)
questions = ['退款政策是什么？', '保修期多久？', '支持哪些支付方式？']
results = await runner.aevaluate_queries(
    index.as_query_engine(), queries=questions)

# 汇总通过率，作为本次改动的基线指标
passed = sum(bool(r.passing) for r in results['faith'])
print(f'faithfulness: {passed}/{len(questions)} passed')
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 三类评估：忠实（防幻觉）、相关（切题）、正确（对参考）。Three checks: faithful (anti-hallucination), relevant (on-topic), correct (vs reference).
  • evaluate_response 直接吃 QueryEngine 的返回（含 source_nodes）。evaluate_response consumes the QueryEngine's response directly (with source_nodes).
  • 评估通常由一个 LLM 充当“裁判”。Evaluation is usually done by an LLM acting as judge.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
评估把 RAG 调优从“凭感觉”变成“可度量的闭环”：改切块、换检索、调 Prompt 后，用同一套指标对比，才知道是真变好了。
Evaluation turns RAG tuning from gut feeling into a measurable loop: after changing chunking, retrieval or prompts, compare on the same metrics to know it actually improved.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. FaithfulnessEvaluator 主要检查什么？What does FaithfulnessEvaluator mainly check?
  1. 答案的语法是否正确Whether the answer's grammar is correct
  2. 检索速度Retrieval speed
  3. 答案是否被检索到的上下文支撑（防幻觉）Whether the answer is supported by the retrieved context (anti-hallucination)
  4. 向量维度Vector dimension
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：CAnswer: C 忠实度衡量答案是否有据可依，是 RAG 防幻觉的核心指标。Faithfulness measures whether the answer is grounded in the context — the core anti-hallucination metric.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你要把调优从“凭感觉”变“可度量闭环”。你会搭什么评估、三把尺子各查什么、各需什么输入？怎么防止“修好一个、悄悄弄坏一批”？You want to turn tuning from 'vibes' into a measurable loop. What evaluation do you set up, what does each of the three rulers measure and need as input, and how do you prevent 'fix one, silently break many'?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：Faithfulness(答案是否忠于检索，需 response+source_nodes)、Relevancy(是否切题，需 query+response+检索上下文)、Correctness(对不对，需参考答案，1–5 分)。闭环：改一处→重测→对比→保留/回退；防回归靠一个固定回归集，每次改动都重跑、看趋势而非单点。🔑 Key: Faithfulness (is the answer grounded in retrieval — needs response + source_nodes), Relevancy (is it on-topic — needs query + response + the retrieved contexts), Correctness (is it right — needs a reference answer, 1–5). The loop: change one thing → re-test → compare → keep/revert; prevent regressions with a fixed regression set re-run on every change, watching trends over single points.
基线 0.82baseline 0.82
→
改 chunk_sizechange chunk_size
→
重测re-test
→
0.71 变差0.71 worse
→ 回退→ revert
→
达标才保留keep only if it holds
可度量闭环：用数字决定保留还是回退，挡住悄悄的退化Measurable loop: numbers decide keep-or-revert, blocking silent regressions
🎯 2. 评估用 LLM-as-judge，有哪些局限？怎么缓解、怎么让分数可信？Evaluation uses LLM-as-judge. What are its limits, and how do you mitigate them to make scores trustworthy?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：judge 本身有噪声/偏见、可能偏向某种风格、成本高、边界判断不稳。缓解：固定 judge 模型与 prompt、用二值/明确 rubric、对关键集做人评校准、看趋势而非单点分数、维护回归集比较相对变化——把它当“相对尺”而非“绝对真值”。🔑 Key: the judge is noisy/biased, may favor a style, costs money, and is shaky on edge cases. Mitigate by pinning the judge model and prompt, using binary/explicit rubrics, calibrating with human review on a key set, watching trends over single scores, and comparing relative change on a fixed set — treat it as a relative ruler, not absolute truth.
🎯 3. 你只有 200 条历史问答、没有标准答案。怎么起步做评估？You have 200 historical Q&A pairs but no reference answers. How do you start evaluating?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：先做不需要参考答案的 Faithfulness 与 Relevancy——它们只看 response/source_nodes/query。Correctness 才需要 reference，可后续对高价值子集人工标注少量 gold 再补。先用前两把尺子建立基线和回归集，立刻就能挡住明显退化。🔑 Key: start with Faithfulness and Relevancy, which need no reference — they look only at response/source_nodes/query. Correctness needs a reference, so hand-label a small gold subset on high-value cases later. The first two rulers establish a baseline and regression set immediately, catching obvious regressions right away.
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 你会如何搭一个最小的回归评估集，防止改动让 RAG 变差？How would you build a minimal regression eval set to keep changes from degrading the RAG?

把整本书拼成一个应用Assembling the whole guide into one app

前 19 课每一课都拆开了管道上的一站；这一课把它们按同一套接口拼回去。整条链路只有两个阶段：写入路径把数据变成可复用、可落盘的索引，查询路径在索引之上反复检索、合成、作答。因为每一站都遵守统一抽象，你可以只替换其中一件（换向量库、换检索器、加一道评估），而不动其余结构。举例：想要更强的召回，把 as_retriever 换成第 18 课的 QueryFusionRetriever 即可，主流程一行不改；而全局 Settings（第 17 课）从一开始就在背后统一着 LLM 与 embedding。
Each of the first 19 lessons opened up one stop on the pipeline; this one snaps them back together behind one shared interface. The whole chain has just two phases: the write path turns data into a reusable, persistable index, and the query path retrieves, synthesizes and answers on top of it — over and over. Because every stop obeys the same abstraction, you can swap a single part (a different vector store, a different retriever, an added evaluator) without disturbing the rest. For example, to boost recall just swap as_retriever for Lesson 18's QueryFusionRetriever — the main flow doesn't change a line; meanwhile the global Settings (Lesson 17) has been unifying the LLM and embedding behind the scenes all along.
首次建库（load → ingest → persist）First build (load → ingest → persist)
首次运行：SimpleDirectoryReader 加载 → IngestionPipeline 切块/抽取 → VectorStoreIndex 向量化建索引 → persist('./storage') 落盘。较重，但只做一次。
First run: SimpleDirectoryReader loads → IngestionPipeline splits/extracts → VectorStoreIndex embeds & indexes → persist('./storage') to disk. Heavy, but one-off.
vs
复用（load_index_from_storage）Reuse (load_index_from_storage)
以后启动：StorageContext.from_defaults(persist_dir='./storage') + load_index_from_storage 直接复活索引，跳过重新切块与向量化，秒级就绪。
Later starts: StorageContext.from_defaults(persist_dir='./storage') + load_index_from_storage revive the index directly — skip re-splitting and re-embedding, ready in seconds.
第一次建库较重；之后用 load_index_from_storage 秒级复用The first build is heavy; afterwards load_index_from_storage reuses it in seconds
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
(综合 / integrates) · VectorStoreIndex · IngestionPipeline · RetrieverQueryEngine · FaithfulnessEvaluator — 把全书组件拼到一起wires the whole guide's components together
深入：端到端组装Deep dive: end-to-end assembly点击展开expand
🧪 示例🧪 Example
capstone 的核心是一个 if os.path.exists(PERSIST) 分支：存在就 load_index_from_storage 秒级复活，否则跑一遍 IngestionPipeline → VectorStoreIndex 再 persist。其余几行只是把检索器、后处理、合成器、评估器装到同一个 RetrieverQueryEngine 上。
The heart of the capstone is one if os.path.exists(PERSIST) branch: if it exists, load_index_from_storage revives it in seconds; otherwise run IngestionPipeline → VectorStoreIndex once, then persist. The remaining lines just bolt a retriever, postprocessor, synthesizer and evaluator onto one RetrieverQueryEngine.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
因为每一站都是实现同一接口的标准件，整台应用才能像搭积木一样拼装。换一个向量库或检索策略时，你不必重写主流程——只把对应那块换掉，RetrieverQueryEngine 的骨架原封不动。
Because every stop is a standard part implementing the same interface, the whole app assembles like building blocks. To change a vector store or retrieval strategy you never rewrite the main flow — just swap that one block while the RetrieverQueryEngine skeleton stays intact.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
运行分两支：首次走写入路径（摄取 → 建索引 → persist），之后走复用路径（load_index_from_storage）。关键时序：Settings.embed_model 必须在建索引之前设好——落盘的向量由它决定，加载后必须用同一个 embedding 才能对齐检索。
It runs in two branches: the first time takes the write path (ingest → index → persist); later runs take the reuse path (load_index_from_storage). Critical ordering: Settings.embed_model must be set before building the index — it determines the vectors written to disk, and after loading you must use the same embedding for retrieval to line up.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
想把这台问答机改造成“带脚注的客服机器人”？只需替换三件：把 query engine 换成 chat_mode='condense_plus_context' 的 chat engine（多轮记忆）、加一道引用后处理把 source_nodes 渲染成脚注、再挂上评估当上线前的质量闸。骨架不变，只换这几块。
Want to turn this answering machine into a “support bot with footnotes”? Swap just three parts: replace the query engine with a chat engine (chat_mode='condense_plus_context') for multi-turn memory, add a citation postprocessor that renders source_nodes as footnotes, and attach evaluation as a pre-launch quality gate. The skeleton stays; only these blocks change.
一个文件跑通完整 RAG（含持久化、后处理、评估、多轮）one file, full RAG: persistence, post-processing, eval, chat
from llama_index.core import (
    SimpleDirectoryReader, VectorStoreIndex, StorageContext,
    load_index_from_storage, Settings, get_response_synthesizer,
)
from llama_index.core.node_parser import SentenceSplitter
from llama_index.core.ingestion import IngestionPipeline
from llama_index.core.postprocessor import SimilarityPostprocessor
from llama_index.core.query_engine import RetrieverQueryEngine
from llama_index.core.evaluation import FaithfulnessEvaluator
from llama_index.llms.openai import OpenAI
from llama_index.embeddings.openai import OpenAIEmbedding
import os

Settings.llm = OpenAI(model='gpt-4o-mini')
Settings.embed_model = OpenAIEmbedding(model='text-embedding-3-small')

PERSIST = './storage'
if os.path.exists(PERSIST):                      # 已建过就秒加载
    index = load_index_from_storage(StorageContext.from_defaults(persist_dir=PERSIST))
else:                                            # 首次：摄取 -> 建索引 -> 落盘
    docs = SimpleDirectoryReader('./data').load_data()
    nodes = IngestionPipeline(transformations=[SentenceSplitter(chunk_size=512, chunk_overlap=50)]).run(documents=docs)
    index = VectorStoreIndex(nodes)
    index.storage_context.persist(persist_dir=PERSIST)

engine = RetrieverQueryEngine.from_args(
    retriever=index.as_retriever(similarity_top_k=4),
    node_postprocessors=[SimilarityPostprocessor(similarity_cutoff=0.4)],  # 阈值随数据而定
    response_synthesizer=get_response_synthesizer(response_mode='compact'),
)
resp = engine.query('退款政策是什么？')
print('答案:', resp)
print('忠实度:', FaithfulnessEvaluator().evaluate_response(response=resp).passing)

chat = index.as_chat_engine(chat_mode='condense_plus_context')
print(chat.chat('那国际订单也一样吗？'))
批量评估当回归测试：改完管道就重跑这套用例Batch eval as a regression test: re-run this set after every pipeline change
from llama_index.core.evaluation import FaithfulnessEvaluator, RelevancyEvaluator

# 在 capstone 的 engine 之上：把单次评估扩成可回归的质量闸
faith = FaithfulnessEvaluator()        # 答案是否忠于检索到的上下文
relev = RelevancyEvaluator()           # 检索到的上下文是否切题

eval_set = ['退款要多久到账？', '国际订单能退吗？', '怎么申请换货？']
passed = 0
for q in eval_set:
    resp = engine.query(q)
    ok = (faith.evaluate_response(response=resp).passing
          and relev.evaluate_response(query=q, response=resp).passing)
    passed += int(ok)
    print(q, 'PASS' if ok else 'FAIL')
print(f'通过率 pass-rate: {passed}/{len(eval_set)}')
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 完整 RAG = 写入路径（建一次、落盘）+ 查询路径（反复问）。A full RAG = write path (build once, persist) + query path (ask repeatedly).
  • 每一站都是可替换组件：换库、换检索、换合成都不动主结构。Every stop is a swappable component: change store/retrieval/synthesis without touching the skeleton.
  • 持久化 + 评估让它从 demo 走向可维护、可回归。Persistence + evaluation take it from demo to maintainable and regression-safe.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
整条管道每一站都能独立替换，却共享统一接口——这正是 LlamaIndex 的核心思想：用可组合的标准件搭出你自己的 RAG。
Every stop swaps independently yet shares one interface — that's LlamaIndex's core idea: compose your own RAG from standard, interchangeable parts.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你要把整套书拼成生产级本地 RAG。首次建库 vs 复用怎么分支？为什么 Settings.embed_model 必须先于建索引？怎么验证整条链路？You're assembling everything into a production-grade local RAG. How do you branch first-build vs reuse, why must Settings.embed_model be set before building the index, and how do you validate the whole chain?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：用 if os.path.exists(PERSIST) 分支(存在→load_index_from_storage，否则建+persist)；embed_model 必须先设，因为落盘向量由它决定、加载后必须同模型才能对齐。设晚或设错→向量在错坐标系，查询报错或相似度全错，只能重建。验证：端到端跑一组问题 + 用 FaithfulnessEvaluator 批量打分，作上线前质量闸。🔑 Key: branch on if os.path.exists(PERSIST) (exists → load_index_from_storage, else build + persist); embed_model must be set first because persisted vectors depend on it and loading must use the same model to line up. Set it late or wrong → vectors in the wrong space, queries error or score nonsensically, fixable only by re-indexing. Validate by running a question set end-to-end plus batch FaithfulnessEvaluator scoring as a pre-launch gate.

🎯 2. 把它改造成“带引用脚注的客服机器人”，你换 / 加哪几件？为什么骨架不用动？To reshape it into a 'support bot with citation footnotes', which parts do you swap or add, and why does the skeleton stay?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：只换/加四件——chat engine(多轮记忆)、引用后处理(把 source_nodes 渲染成脚注)、收紧 prompt(只引用)、评估闸。因为每一站都遵守统一接口、正交可替换，写入/查询主干(QueryEngine 装配)原封不动——这正是“可组合标准件”的红利。🔑 Key: swap/add just four — a chat engine (memory), a citation postprocessor (render source_nodes as footnotes), a tightened cite-only prompt, and an evaluation gate. Because every stop obeys one interface and is orthogonally swappable, the write/query backbone (the QueryEngine assembly) stays untouched — exactly the dividend of 'composable standard parts'.
🎯 3. 面试官说“一句话讲清 LlamaIndex 的 RAG 核心思想”。你会怎么答？The interviewer asks: 'in one sentence, the core idea of LlamaIndex RAG'. What's your answer?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：RAG 是一条由可组合标准件搭成的数据管道——写入路径把知识外置成可检索、可更新、可溯源的索引，查询路径在其上据此作答，每一站都遵守统一接口、可独立替换与评估。加分点：能顺势举一个“替换某一站”的例子(换向量库/加 rerank/接 chat)说明它的可组合性。🔑 Key: RAG is a data pipeline of composable standard parts — the write path externalizes knowledge into a searchable, refreshable, citable index, and the query path answers from it, with every stop sharing one interface and independently swappable and measurable. Bonus: follow up with a 'swap one stop' example (change the vector store / add a reranker / attach chat) to show the composability.

  • 如果知识库有上百万文档，写入路径与查询路径各自最先遇到的瓶颈是什么？With millions of documents, what's the first bottleneck on the write path vs the query path?
第六部分 · 生产进阶

21 · 生产级检索

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

到了生产环境，朴素 top-k 的“一路向量、直接取前 k”常常不够：精确编号查不准、罕见词召不回、真正相关的排在后面。生产级检索的标准答案是混合检索（向量 + BM25 两路召回）+ Rerank 精排，必要时再加 HyDE 改写——核心是把召回和精度分两步拿。In production, naive top-k — one vector path, take the first k — often isn't enough: exact ids miss, rare words don't get recalled, and the truly relevant hits rank too low. The standard answer is hybrid retrieval (vector + BM25 dual recall) + reranking, plus HyDE rewriting when needed — the core idea is to get recall and precision in two separate steps.

问题Question
→
向量检索 · BM25Vector · BM25
两路各取 top-10（宁可多召）top-10 each (over-fetch)
→
融合 (RRF)Fuse (RRF)
倒数排名累加、去重reciprocal-rank, deduped
→
Rerank 精排Rerank
交叉编码器逐条打分cross-encoder re-scores
→
top-3top-3
最相关的几条进 promptthe few best into the prompt
先广召回，再精排：向量 + BM25 两路召回 → RRF 融合 → rerank 精排 → top-3Recall broad, then rerank narrow: vector + BM25 recall → RRF fusion → rerank → top-3
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
像招聘：先广撒网多收简历（混合召回，宁可多别漏），再让资深面试官逐份细看挑出最合适的几个（rerank 精排）——海选要全，终面要准。
Like hiring: first cast a wide net for résumés (hybrid recall — over-collect, never miss), then let a senior interviewer read each closely and pick the best few (rerank) — screening wants completeness, the final round wants precision.

混合检索：向量懂语义，BM25 补字面Hybrid retrieval: vectors for meaning, BM25 for the letter

对比项Aspect纯向量检索Vector-onlyBM25（关键词）BM25 (keyword)混合 + RerankHybrid + Rerank
核心机制Mechanismembedding 语义近邻semantic nearest-neighbor词频 / 精确匹配term-frequency / exact match两路召回 → 交叉编码器精排dual recall → cross-encoder rerank
擅长Strong at近义、改写、换种问法synonyms, rephrasings, paraphrase精确编号、罕见词、专有名词exact ids, rare words, proper nouns语义 + 字面都覆盖both meaning and letter
盲区Blind spot精确符号“X-2000”可能漏may miss an exact symbol like “X-2000”读不懂同义改写blind to synonymy / paraphrase多一步算力，更慢更贵one extra step — slower, pricier

为什么生产 RAG 几乎都要混合检索 + RerankWhy production RAG almost always needs hybrid retrieval + rerank

纯向量检索懂语义——近义、换种问法都能命中，但它把文本压成一个语义向量，对精确 token 和罕见词（产品编号、报错码、专有名词）不敏感，这类查询常常排不进 top-k。BM25 正好相反：按字面词频匹配，精确编号一击即中，却读不懂同义改写。于是生产里把两路并联召回、用 RRF 融合，语义与字面互补。但召回求“全”难免带进噪声，所以再加一层 rerank：用交叉编码器把 query 和每个候选放在一起重新打分，把真正相关的提到最前——召回与精度分两步拿，这就是几乎所有生产 RAG 的检索骨架。
Pure vector search understands meaning — synonyms and rephrasings still hit — but it squeezes text into one semantic vector and is weak on exact tokens and rare words (product ids, error codes, proper nouns), so such queries often fall out of top-k. BM25 is the mirror image: it matches literal term frequency, nailing an exact id but blind to synonymy. So production runs both paths in parallel and fuses them with RRF, letting meaning and letter complement each other. Recall chasing completeness inevitably drags in noise, so a rerank layer follows: a cross-encoder scores the query and each candidate together, lifting the truly relevant to the top — getting recall and precision in two separate steps, the retrieval backbone of nearly every production RAG.
纯向量检索Vector-only
问“X-2000 的保修期”，embedding 把它读成“某型号保修”，却对精确编号 X-2000 不敏感——相关条款排在第 12 名，进不了 top-5，答案只能靠猜。
Ask “warranty of X-2000” and the embedding reads it as “warranty of some model”, blind to the exact id X-2000 — the right clause ranks #12, never enters top-5, and the answer is a guess.
vs
混合检索 + RerankHybrid + Rerank
BM25 直接按字面命中含 X-2000 的那一条，和向量召回一起进候选池；rerank 再把真正写明保修期的那条提到第 1——精确编号不再漏。
BM25 hits the line literally containing X-2000 and joins the vector candidates in the pool; rerank then lifts the clause that actually states the warranty to #1 — the exact id is never missed again.
同一个查询：纯向量漏掉精确编号，混合用 BM25 补回字面匹配再精排Same query: vector-only misses the exact id; hybrid adds BM25's literal match, then reranks

RRF 用 1/(k+rank) 累加两路排名——只在一路强的条款也能浮上来（✓ = 进入最终 top-k）RRF sums 1/(k+rank) across both paths — a clause strong in only one path still surfaces (✓ = kept in the final top-k)

再进一步：HyDE 用“假设答案”贴近文档Going further: HyDE uses a “hypothetical answer” to match the docs

混合检索和 rerank 解决“召回 + 精排”，HyDE（Hypothetical Document Embeddings）则换个角度提升召回：先让 LLM 根据问题写一段假设答案，再用这段更像文档的文本去做向量检索。短问句和文档措辞往往对不齐，而“假设答案”天然贴近文档语气，召回常常更准。
Hybrid retrieval and rerank handle recall-plus-rerank; HyDE (Hypothetical Document Embeddings) lifts recall from another angle: let the LLM first draft a hypothetical answer to the question, then run vector search with that doc-like text. Terse questions rarely match document wording, but a hypothetical answer naturally echoes the document's tone, so recall is often better.
原始问句Raw question
“远程办公要审批吗？”“need approval to WFH?”
→
LLM 写假设答案LLM drafts a hypothetical
一段像文档的回答a doc-like passage
→
用假设答案检索Retrieve with it
它的向量更贴文档措辞its vector matches doc wording
→
命中更准Better hits
召回贴近政策原文recall closer to the policy text
HyDE：先让 LLM 写个“假设答案”，再用它的向量去检索——往往比用问句本身更贴文档措辞HyDE: let the LLM draft a hypothetical answer, then search with its vector — often closer to the document's wording than the question
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
retrievers/fusion_retriever.py · QueryFusionRetriever — 把多路检索器用 RRF 融合成一路（混合检索的核心）fuses multiple retrievers into one via RRF (the heart of hybrid retrieval)
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
llama-index-retrievers-bm25 · BM25Retriever — 关键词 / 精确 token 检索，作为向量之外的另一路召回（独立集成包）keyword / exact-token retrieval as the second recall path beside vectors (a separate integration package)
深入：混合检索、RRF 与 Rerank 的取舍Deep dive: hybrid retrieval, RRF and the rerank trade-offs点击展开expand
🧪 示例：装配“混合 + 精排”一条链🧪 Example: wiring a hybrid + rerank chain
两路召回各取 top-10：index.as_retriever() 走向量，BM25Retriever.from_defaults(docstore=index.docstore) 走关键词；用 QueryFusionRetriever([vector, bm25], mode='reciprocal_rerank') 融合，再把 CohereRerank(top_n=3) 作为 node_postprocessor 精排到 3 条。
Two recall paths, top-10 each: index.as_retriever() for vectors and BM25Retriever.from_defaults(docstore=index.docstore) for keywords; fuse with QueryFusionRetriever([vector, bm25], mode='reciprocal_rerank'), then add CohereRerank(top_n=3) as a node_postprocessor to narrow to 3.
❓ 为什么这么设计❓ Why designed this way
一步到位很难同时做到“全”和“准”。生产 RAG 索性解耦：召回阶段只求别漏（向量 + BM25 多路、each top-10~20，宁可多召），精排阶段只求排得准（rerank 用更贵的交叉编码器在小候选集上细判）。两步各自优化，比单一相似度分数既快又准。
One pass can't be both complete and precise, so production RAG decouples them: the recall stage only avoids misses (vector + BM25, top-10~20 each, over-fetch on purpose), and the rerank stage only gets the order right (a pricier cross-encoder judges the small candidate set). Optimizing each step separately beats a single similarity score on both speed and accuracy.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑⚙️ How it runs inside
QueryFusionRetriever 把每路结果按倒数排名（RRF）累加打分再合并去重，num_queries=1 表示不改写问句、只融合多个检索器；rerank 不在检索器里，而是作为 node_postprocessor 挂在 QueryEngine 上，对融合后的候选逐条用 query+doc 一起打分、取 top-n。
QueryFusionRetriever merges each path's results by reciprocal rank (RRF), deduping as it goes; num_queries=1 means don't rewrite the query, just fuse the retrievers. Rerank lives not in the retriever but as a node_postprocessor on the QueryEngine, scoring each fused candidate with query+doc together and keeping the top-n.
🔀 替代方案🔀 Alternatives
精排器可换：CohereRerank（托管 API，最省事最准，但按调用计费且数据出网）、本地 SentenceTransformer 交叉编码器（SentenceTransformerRerank，数据不出网、免调用费，但要本地 GPU/算力）、LLMRerank（让 LLM 直接判相关性，最灵活但最慢最贵）。按数据合规、延迟预算和成本三角去选。
The reranker is swappable: CohereRerank (hosted API — easiest and most accurate, but billed per call and data leaves your network), a local SentenceTransformer cross-encoder (SentenceTransformerRerank — data stays in, no per-call fee, but needs local GPU/compute), and LLMRerank (an LLM judges relevance directly — most flexible but slowest and priciest). Pick along the data-compliance / latency / cost triangle.
生产配方：向量 + BM25 两路召回 → RRF 融合 → Cohere 精排 top-3Production recipe: vector + BM25 recall → RRF fusion → Cohere rerank to top-3
from llama_index.core.retrievers import QueryFusionRetriever
from llama_index.core.query_engine import RetrieverQueryEngine
from llama_index.retrievers.bm25 import BM25Retriever            # pip install llama-index-retrievers-bm25
from llama_index.postprocessor.cohere_rerank import CohereRerank  # pip install llama-index-postprocessor-cohere-rerank

# 两路召回：向量(语义) + BM25(精确 token)，先各取 10
vector = index.as_retriever(similarity_top_k=10)
bm25 = BM25Retriever.from_defaults(docstore=index.docstore, similarity_top_k=10)

# 用 reciprocal-rank fusion 融合两路（num_queries=1 表示不改写、只融合检索器）
hybrid = QueryFusionRetriever([vector, bm25], num_queries=1,
                              similarity_top_k=10, mode='reciprocal_rerank')

# 再用 rerank 模型把 10 条精排到最相关的 3 条（需 COHERE_API_KEY）
engine = RetrieverQueryEngine.from_args(
    retriever=hybrid, node_postprocessors=[CohereRerank(top_n=3)])
print(engine.query('X-2000 的保修期是多久？'))
HyDE：先写“假设答案”，再用它的向量检索——更贴文档措辞HyDE: draft a hypothetical answer, then retrieve with its vector — closer to the doc's wording
from llama_index.core.indices.query.query_transform import HyDEQueryTransform
from llama_index.core.query_engine import TransformQueryEngine

# HyDE：先让 LLM 写一个“假设答案”，用它的向量去检索——往往比用问句本身更贴近文档措辞
hyde = HyDEQueryTransform(include_original=True)
engine = TransformQueryEngine(index.as_query_engine(similarity_top_k=5), query_transform=hyde)
print(engine.query('远程办公需要审批吗？'))
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 生产检索 = 广召回（向量 + BM25 混合）+ 精排（rerank），召回与精度分两步拿。Production retrieval = broad recall (vector + BM25 hybrid) + precise rerank — recall and precision in two steps.
  • 纯向量对精确编号 / 罕见词不敏感；BM25 补字面匹配，二者用 RRF 融合。Vectors miss exact ids / rare tokens; BM25 adds literal matching, fused via RRF.
  • Rerank 是 node_postprocessor（不是检索器），用交叉编码器把真正相关的提前。Rerank is a node_postprocessor (not a retriever) — a cross-encoder that lifts the truly relevant ones.
  • HyDE 用“假设答案”的向量检索，往往比原问句更贴文档措辞。HyDE retrieves with a hypothetical answer's vector, often closer to the document's wording than the raw question.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
生产检索的精髓是把召回和精度拆开：先用混合检索“宁可多召、别漏”，再用 rerank“在小候选集里排得准”——一步求全、一步求准，比单一相似度分数又快又稳。
The essence of production retrieval is splitting recall from precision: hybrid retrieval first (over-fetch, never miss), then rerank (order the small candidate set precisely) — one step for completeness, one for correctness, beating a single similarity score on both speed and reliability.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. 纯向量检索为什么会漏掉精确编号“X-2000”这样的查询？Why can pure vector search miss an exact id like 'X-2000'?
  1. embedding 偏语义，对精确符号/罕见 token 不敏感，可能排不进 top-kembeddings capture meaning and are weak on exact symbols/rare tokens, so it may miss top-k
  2. top_k 一定太小top_k is always too small
  3. 向量库坏了the vector store is broken
  4. 必须重建索引you must re-index
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：AAnswer: A 解决靠混合检索(向量 + BM25/关键词)或把编号写进 metadata 精确过滤。Fix with hybrid retrieval (vector + BM25) or exact metadata filtering.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 线上客服 RAG 要加一道 rerank 精排。你会在 Cohere 托管、本地 SentenceTransformer 交叉编码器、LLMRerank 之间怎么选？数据合规、延迟、成本各自怎么权衡，又怎么验证 rerank 真的有用？Your live support RAG needs a rerank step. How do you choose among hosted Cohere, a local SentenceTransformer cross-encoder, and LLMRerank? How do you weigh data compliance, latency and cost, and how do you verify rerank actually helps?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：三者是“准确 / 成本 / 是否本地”的取舍——Cohere 最省事最准，但数据出网且按调用计费；本地 SentenceTransformer 数据不出网、免调用费，但要 GPU；LLMRerank 最灵活却最慢最贵。合规敏感（医疗/金融）优先本地；要开箱即用且数据可外发选 Cohere；只在高价值、可容忍延迟的少量查询上才考虑 LLMRerank。验证：固定一组 gold 查询，比较“仅向量 / 混合 / 混合+rerank”三档的命中率与端到端答案质量，再核对每条新增的延迟与单价是否值得。🔑 Key: the three trade off accuracy / cost / on-prem — Cohere is easiest and most accurate but data leaves the network and is billed per call; a local SentenceTransformer keeps data in and is fee-free but needs a GPU; LLMRerank is most flexible yet slowest and priciest. For compliance-sensitive domains (health/finance) prefer local; for plug-and-play with data allowed to egress pick Cohere; reserve LLMRerank for a few high-value, latency-tolerant queries. Verify on a fixed gold set: compare hit-rate and end-to-end answer quality across vector-only / hybrid / hybrid+rerank, then check whether the added latency and per-call cost are worth it.

三种 rerank 的取舍：准确 / 成本 / 是否本地——按数据合规与延迟预算选Three rerankers traded off on accuracy / cost / on-prem — choose by data compliance and latency budget
🎯 2. 用户报“问产品编号 X-2000 的保修期，答得驴唇不对马嘴”。纯向量为什么会漏？你会怎么修，为什么不是直接把 top_k 调大？Users report “asking the warranty for product id X-2000 gives a nonsense answer”. Why does pure vector miss it, how would you fix it, and why not just raise top_k?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：embedding 偏语义，对精确符号/罕见 token（如 X-2000）不敏感，相关条款可能排在很后面、进不了 top-k——这是“字面匹配”问题，不是“召回量”问题。调大 top_k 只是把噪声一起拉进来、更慢更贵，真正该补的是字面那一路：加 BM25 做混合检索，让精确编号被直接命中，再用 RRF 融合 + rerank 精排；或把编号写进 metadata 做精确过滤。验证：在含编号的 gold 查询上比较修复前后的命中率。🔑 Key: embeddings capture meaning and are weak on exact symbols/rare tokens (like X-2000), so the right clause can rank far down and never enter top-k — a literal-match problem, not a recall-volume one. Raising top_k just drags in noise, slower and pricier; the real fix is the literal path: add BM25 for hybrid retrieval so the exact id is hit directly, fuse via RRF and rerank; or write the id into metadata for exact filtering. Verify by comparing hit-rate before/after on id-bearing gold queries.
🎯 3. 有人提议给检索加 HyDE。它的原理是什么、什么场景最有效、又有什么风险？你怎么决定上不上？Someone proposes adding HyDE to retrieval. How does it work, when does it help most, what's the risk, and how do you decide whether to adopt it?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：HyDE 先让 LLM 写一个“假设答案”，用这段更像文档的文本的向量去检索——当问句很短、措辞和文档差距大时，召回往往明显变好。风险：多一次 LLM 调用（更慢更贵），且假设答案若跑偏会把检索带偏（垃圾进、垃圾出）；所以 include_original=True 保留原问句一起检索更稳。决定上不上：在 gold 集上对比 HyDE 前后的命中率与端到端质量，再权衡多出的延迟/成本是否值得。🔑 Key: HyDE first has the LLM draft a “hypothetical answer”, then retrieves with that doc-like text's vector — when questions are terse and worded unlike the documents, recall often improves clearly. Risks: an extra LLM call (slower, pricier) and, if the hypothetical drifts, it can steer retrieval astray (garbage in, garbage out) — so include_original=True keeps the raw question in the mix for safety. Decide by comparing hit-rate and end-to-end quality with/without HyDE on a gold set, then weigh the added latency/cost.
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 你的查询里既有自然语言问题也有精确产品编号，你会怎么配比向量与关键词两路的权重？With both natural-language questions and exact product ids in your queries, how would you weight the vector vs keyword paths?
第六部分 · 生产进阶

22 · 规模化评估与 CI 闸

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

L19 学会了给单个答案打分；到了生产和团队协作，评估必须规模化、还要自动守门。三件事：① 用 DatasetGenerator 从文档自动造一批金标问题（再人工挑高价值子集标注）；② 用 BatchEvalRunner 并发批量跑几十上百题、聚合成一个通过率；③ 把通过率接进 CI 做回归闸——低于阈值就 fail，坏改动合不进主干。一句话：把“凭感觉调”升级成“分数门槛守门”。L19 taught you to score a single answer; in production and on a team, evaluation must scale and gate automatically. Three moves: (1) use DatasetGenerator to auto-build a batch of gold questions from your docs (then hand-label a high-value subset); (2) use BatchEvalRunner to run dozens-to-hundreds of them concurrently and aggregate into one pass-rate; (3) wire that pass-rate into CI as a regression gate — below threshold the build fails and the bad change can't reach main. In a line: upgrade “tune by feel” into “a score threshold guards the door”.

金标集 → 批量评估 → 聚合 → 守门：分数达标才让改动进主干，不达标自动拦回Gold set → batch eval → aggregate → gate: only a passing score lets a change into main; a failing one is blocked automatically
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
像工厂出货前的自动质检关：每批货（每次改动）都要过同一组固定抽检（回归金标集），合格才放行上线（合并主干），不合格当场拦下（回退）。检验标准事先定死、机器自动判，没人能靠“感觉还行”把次品偷偷放出去。
Like an automated QC gate before shipping: every batch (each change) must pass the same fixed sample inspection (the regression gold set); only a pass ships (merges to main), a fail is stopped on the spot (revert). The spec is fixed in advance and a machine rules on it — nobody can sneak a defect through on “feels fine”.

同样三把尺子，关键看“在哪跑”：免参考的忠实/相关当 CI 闸主力，需参考答案的正确性留给人工金标子集离线跑Same three rulers — what matters is “where they run”: reference-free faithfulness/relevancy power the CI gate, while reference-needing correctness runs offline over a human gold subset

从“手动评一次”到“自动守门”From “evaluate once by hand” to “gate automatically”

金标从哪来Where gold comes from临时想几个问题invent a few questions on the spotDatasetGenerator 自动造 + 人工标注高价值子集，沉淀为固定回归集DatasetGenerator auto-builds + a human-labeled high-value subset, hardened into a fixed regression set
何时触发When it runs改完想起来才跑一次run once, if you remember每次 PR/提交在 CI 自动跑（pytest 脚本）every PR/commit, automatically in CI (a pytest script)
不达标怎样On a miss自己看一眼、容易忘you glance at it, easy to forgetassert 失败、构建变红、挡住合并assert fails, the build goes red, merge blocked
防的风险Risk it guards只知这次改动好不好only whether this one change is OK“修一个坏一批”的悄悄回归the silent “fix one, break many” regression

把“凭感觉调”变成“分数门槛守门”Turning “tune by feel” into “a score threshold guards the door”

评估要当“闸”用，前提是有一套稳定、可复跑的金标集。从零造太慢，所以先自动起步：DatasetGenerator 按文档块批量生成问题，几分钟就能铺出几十上百题的基线。但自动题良莠不齐，于是再做一层人工策展：挑出高价值、易回归的场景，补上人工核对的参考答案，沉淀成一个越用越准的回归子集。有了固定金标集，每次改动都对同一批题重跑、比趋势——这正是挡住“修一个坏一批”的关键：你盯着的那道题修好了，分数却告诉你另外十道悄悄退化了。最后把“低于阈值就 fail”写进 CI，守门这件事就不再依赖人的自觉。
Using evaluation as a gate requires a stable, re-runnable gold set. Building one from scratch is slow, so start automatically: DatasetGenerator mass-produces questions per document chunk, laying down a dozens-to-hundreds baseline in minutes. But auto-generated questions are uneven, so add a layer of human curation: pick the high-value, regression-prone scenarios, attach human-checked reference answers, and let them harden into a regression subset that grows more trustworthy with use. With a fixed gold set, every change re-runs against the same questions and you watch the trend — exactly what blocks “fix one, break many”: the case you were staring at got fixed, but the score tells you ten others quietly regressed. Finally write “below threshold → fail” into CI, and gatekeeping no longer depends on anyone's discipline.

金标集的造与养：自动起量 → 人工提纯 → 补参考答案 → 固化回归集 → 线上真实问题持续回灌Building and maintaining the gold set: auto for volume → human refine → add references → freeze a regression set → keep feeding real production questions

一道闸怎么挡住“修一个坏一批”How one gate blocks “fix one, break many”

回归闸的价值不在“这次改得好不好”，而在“别处有没有被悄悄带坏”。把同一套金标接进 CI，单题的局部改进再也盖不住整体的退化——分数跌破阈值，改动就进不了主干。
A regression gate's value isn't “is this change good?” but “did it quietly break something elsewhere?”. Wire the same gold set into CI and a local single-question win can no longer mask an overall regression — break the threshold and the change can't reach main.
没有回归闸（手动）No gate (manual)
为修好“退款多久到账”这道投诉，把 chunk_size 从 512 调到 1024。本地一看那题确实顺了就合并——可“保修期”“发票抬头”等十几道题的忠实度悄悄从 0.92 掉到 0.78，没人察觉，线上开始答非所问。
To fix one complaint — “how long do refunds take” — you bump chunk_size from 512 to 1024. Locally that one reads fine, so you merge — but a dozen others (“warranty period”, “invoice title”) quietly drop in faithfulness from 0.92 to 0.78, unnoticed, and production starts answering off-topic.
vs
有 CI 回归闸With a CI gate
同样的改动推上 PR，CI 用 50 题金标集并发重跑：那道题虽好，但整体通过率 0.92 → 0.78、跌破 0.90 阈值，assert 失败、构建变红，PR 合不进主干——“修一个坏一批”当场被拦。
Push the same change as a PR and CI re-runs the 50-question gold set concurrently: that one improved, but the overall pass-rate 0.92 → 0.78 breaks the 0.90 bar, assert fails, the build goes red, and the PR can't reach main — “fix one, break many” is caught on the spot.
同一次改动：没有闸，单题修好却悄悄拖垮十几题；有 CI 闸，整体通过率跌破阈值就当场拦回Same change: without a gate one fix silently drags down a dozen others; with a CI gate, the overall pass-rate breaking the bar blocks it on the spot
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
evaluation/batch_runner.py · BatchEvalRunner — 把多个评估器、多道问题并发批量跑，聚合成可对比的分数（规模化评估的核心）runs many evaluators over many questions concurrently, aggregating comparable scores (the heart of evaluation at scale)
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
evaluation/dataset_generation.py · DatasetGenerator — 从文档自动生成 QA 金标问题，作为回归集的起点（再人工策展）。注：本版 core(0.14.22) 中 DatasetGenerator 已标记 deprecated（源码提示用 RagDatasetGenerator 替代），但该后继类此版 core 尚未内置；这里仍用它，因为它是 core 内唯一的数据集生成器。auto-generates gold QA questions from documents as a starting regression set (then human-curated). Note: in this core build (0.14.22) DatasetGenerator is marked deprecated (the source points to RagDatasetGenerator as its replacement), but that successor isn't shipped in this core build; we still use it here because it is the only dataset generator in core.
深入：造金标集、批量评估与 CI 闸的取舍Deep dive: building the gold set, batch eval and the CI-gate trade-offs点击展开expand
🧪 示例：造一批金标、并发批量评🧪 Example: build a gold batch, evaluate concurrently
DatasetGenerator.from_documents(docs, num_questions_per_chunk=2) 先按块批量出题，.generate_questions_from_nodes() 拿到一串问题；再交给 BatchEvalRunner({'faithfulness': ..., 'relevancy': ...}, workers=8) 的 aevaluate_queries(engine, queries=...) 并发跑完，结果按指标名分组、每题一个 EvaluationResult。
DatasetGenerator.from_documents(docs, num_questions_per_chunk=2) mass-produces questions per chunk, .generate_questions_from_nodes() yields the list; hand them to BatchEvalRunner({'faithfulness': ..., 'relevancy': ...}, workers=8)'s aevaluate_queries(engine, queries=...) to run concurrently — results grouped by metric name, one EvaluationResult per question.
❓ 为什么这么设计（可度量闭环）❓ Why designed this way (a measurable loop)
L19 把单次改动变得“可度量”，生产要的是让度量自动守门。把通过率接进 CI，坏改动在合并前就被分数拦下，质量不再依赖谁记得手动跑评估——“修一个坏一批”的回归被一道常态化的闸挡住。免参考的忠实度/相关性最适合当这道闸（不需要参考答案、能完全自动化）。
L19 made one change “measurable”; production wants the measurement to gate automatically. Wire pass-rate into CI and a bad change is blocked by the score before merge — quality no longer depends on who remembers to run evals by hand, and the “fix one, break many” regression is held back by a standing gate. Reference-free faithfulness/relevancy fit this gate best (no gold answers needed, fully automatable).
⚙️ 内部怎么跑（并发 · EvaluationResult.passing）⚙️ How it runs inside (concurrency · EvaluationResult.passing)
BatchEvalRunner 用 workers 控制并发度，底层走 async：先用 QueryEngine 批量产生答案，再把每个 (query, response, source_nodes) 喂给各评估器（多为 LLM-as-judge）。返回是 dict[str, list[EvaluationResult]]，每个 EvaluationResult 带 passing（是否达标）与 score；把一列 passing 求平均就是通过率，CI 闸比的就是它。
BatchEvalRunner uses workers to set concurrency, async under the hood: it first batch-produces answers via the QueryEngine, then feeds each (query, response, source_nodes) to the evaluators (mostly LLM-as-judge). It returns a dict[str, list[EvaluationResult]]; each EvaluationResult carries passing (met the bar) and score — averaging a column of passing gives the pass-rate the CI gate compares against.
🔀 替代方案（自动生成 vs 人工标注 vs 线上反馈）🔀 Alternatives (auto-gen vs human labeling vs prod feedback)
金标从哪来，有三条路：自动生成（DatasetGenerator，最快铺量，但题目参差、可能问得很浅）；人工标注（最准、能给参考答案支撑 Correctness，但慢且贵，只配给高价值子集）；线上真实反馈（用户点踩、人工申诉、客服转人工的会话——最贴近真实分布，但要脱敏与清洗）。生产里三者叠用：自动起量、人工提纯、线上补真实长尾。
Gold data comes from three sources: auto-generation (DatasetGenerator — fastest to scale, but uneven and often shallow questions); human labeling (most accurate, supplies the reference answers Correctness needs, but slow and costly — reserve it for a high-value subset); and real production feedback (thumbs-down, escalations, handed-off chats — closest to the true distribution, but needs redaction and cleanup). Production stacks all three: auto for volume, humans for purity, production for the real long tail.
造集 + 并发批量评估：DatasetGenerator 自动出题 → BatchEvalRunner（workers=8）并发跑 50 题Build the set + batch-evaluate concurrently: DatasetGenerator drafts questions → BatchEvalRunner (workers=8) runs 50 in parallel
from llama_index.core.evaluation import (DatasetGenerator, BatchEvalRunner,
                                         FaithfulnessEvaluator, RelevancyEvaluator)

# 1) 自动造金标问题（生产里再人工挑选/标注更可靠的子集）
questions = DatasetGenerator.from_documents(
    docs, num_questions_per_chunk=2).generate_questions_from_nodes()

# 2) 并发批量评估：忠实度 + 相关性
runner = BatchEvalRunner(
    {'faithfulness': FaithfulnessEvaluator(), 'relevancy': RelevancyEvaluator()}, workers=8)
results = await runner.aevaluate_queries(index.as_query_engine(), queries=questions[:50])
把通过率变成 CI 回归闸：低于阈值就 assert 失败、挡住合并Turn pass-rate into a CI regression gate: below threshold, assert fails and the merge is blocked
# 把评估变成 CI 回归闸：均通过率低于阈值就 fail（放进 pytest / CI 脚本）
def pass_rate(rs):
    return sum(r.passing for r in rs) / len(rs)

faith = pass_rate(results['faithfulness'])
print(f'faithfulness pass-rate: {faith:.0%}')
assert faith >= 0.9, '忠实度回退，拦截本次变更'   # 守门：不达标就别合并
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 规模化评估 = 自动造金标（DatasetGenerator）+ 并发批量评（BatchEvalRunner）+ CI 回归闸（通过率阈值），把评估从手动升级成自动守门。Evaluation at scale = auto-built gold (DatasetGenerator) + concurrent batch eval (BatchEvalRunner) + a CI regression gate (pass-rate threshold) — manual evaluation upgraded to automatic gatekeeping.
  • 固定回归金标集是闸的前提：自动生成起量、人工标注高价值子集，挡住“修一个坏一批”。A fixed regression gold set is the gate's prerequisite: auto-generate for volume, hand-label a high-value subset — blocking “fix one, break many”.
  • BatchEvalRunner 用 workers 并发跑、按指标聚合 EvaluationResult.passing；通过率就是闸比对的数。BatchEvalRunner runs concurrently via workers and aggregates EvaluationResult.passing per metric; the pass-rate is what the gate compares.
  • 免参考的忠实/相关最适合当 CI 闸；正确性需参考答案，留给人工金标子集。Reference-free faithfulness/relevancy fit the CI gate best; correctness needs references — reserve it for the human gold subset.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
规模化评估的精髓是把“评估”变成“闸”：一套固定可复跑的金标集 + 一个通过率阈值，让每次改动都必须用同一把尺子自证没有变差——质量从“谁记得测”升级成“不达标就合不进来”。
The essence of evaluation at scale is turning “evaluation” into a gate: a fixed, re-runnable gold set plus a pass-rate threshold forces every change to prove — against the same ruler — that it didn't regress; quality goes from “whoever remembers to test” to “below the bar, it can't get in”.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. 把固定的回归金标集接进 CI 闸，最关键的作用是？Wiring a fixed regression gold set into a CI gate matters most because it…
  1. 让单次回答的分数更高makes a single answer score higher
  2. 让评估不再需要 LLMremoves the need for an LLM in evaluation
  3. 彻底取代人工标注fully replaces human labeling
  4. 用同一批题重跑，挡住“修好一个却悄悄弄坏一批”的回归re-runs the same questions to block “fix one, silently break many” regressions
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：DAnswer: D 回归集的价值在“同一批题、每次重跑、比趋势”：你盯的那题修好了，分数还能告诉你别的题有没有悄悄退化；达不到阈值就 fail，坏改动合不进主干。A regression set's value is “same questions, re-run every time, watch the trend”: the case you fixed may pass while others quietly regress, and the score reveals it; below threshold it fails, so the bad change can't reach main.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你要给一套上线的 RAG 建 CI 质量闸。金标集怎么造、阈值怎么定、judge 误判了怎么办？又怎么验证这道闸本身有效（不是摆设、也不会动不动误杀）？You're building a CI quality gate for a live RAG. How do you build the gold set, set the threshold, handle judge misfires, and how do you verify the gate itself works (neither a rubber stamp nor a flaky blocker)?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：金标集先自动生成起量、再人工策展高价值子集；阈值用基线分布定、且只卡“相对回退”；judge 误判靠固定 judge+rubric、看趋势、留容忍带；闸的有效性要拿“已知好/坏改动”去回归测试它。① 造集：DatasetGenerator 自动铺几十上百题，人工挑高价值、易回归的场景补参考答案，沉淀成固定回归集；② 定阈值：先跑基线得到通过率分布，阈值卡在“比基线明显下降”（如低于基线 5 个点就 fail），而非拍一个绝对数；③ 误判：固定 judge 模型与 prompt、用二值 rubric、对边界样本人评校准，关注整体通过率趋势而非单题抖动；④ 验证闸本身：故意提交一个已知会变差的改动（把 chunk 改坏 / 砍掉 rerank），闸必须变红；再提交一个已知无害的改动，闸必须放行——闸也要回归测试，否则它只是个绿灯摆设。🔑 Key: auto-generate the gold set for volume then human-curate a high-value subset; set the threshold from the baseline distribution and gate on relative regression; tame judge misfires with a pinned judge+rubric, trends and a tolerance band; and prove the gate works by regression-testing it with known-good/known-bad changes. (1) Build: DatasetGenerator lays down dozens-to-hundreds, then hand-pick high-value, regression-prone cases and add reference answers, hardening a fixed regression set; (2) threshold: run a baseline for the pass-rate distribution and gate on “clearly below baseline” (e.g. fail if it drops 5 points), not an arbitrary absolute number; (3) misfires: pin the judge model and prompt, use a binary rubric, calibrate edge cases with human review, and watch the overall pass-rate trend rather than single-question jitter; (4) verify the gate: deliberately submit a known-bad change (break chunking / drop the reranker) and the gate must go red, then a known-harmless one and it must pass — the gate itself needs regression testing, or it's just a green rubber stamp.

一次 CI 闸触发：通过率从基线 0.93 跌到 0.86、低于 0.90 阈值，PR 被自动拦回One gate trip: pass-rate falls from baseline 0.93 to 0.86, under the 0.90 bar — the PR is auto-blocked
🎯 2. 有同事说“金标集直接用 DatasetGenerator 自动生成就行，省得人工标注”。你同意吗？自动题有什么坑，你会怎么把这套金标做得可信、可长期当闸用？A teammate says “just auto-generate the gold set with DatasetGenerator — skip human labeling”. Do you agree? What are the pitfalls of auto-generated gold, and how would you make the set trustworthy enough to gate on long-term?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：自动生成适合“快速起量”，但不能直接当唯一金标——它问得浅、可能脱离真实分布，还无法支撑需要参考答案的 Correctness。坑：① 题目多是“文档里直接抄得到”的浅问，测不出真实难例；② 分布偏向文档密集处，真实高频问法反而漏；③ 没有人工核对的参考答案，Correctness 用不了，且自动题里混着噪声会让闸“误判”。做可信：自动生成只当草稿池，人工挑选 + 改写 + 标注出一个高价值子集，再掺入线上真实问题（点踩/转人工的会话）补真实长尾；CI 闸主要用免参考的忠实/相关跑全量草稿、用人工金标子集跑 Correctness。怎么验证金标本身够好：让它能区分已知的好坏配置（好配置分明显更高），区分不出就说明题目没区分度，得继续提纯。🔑 Key: auto-generation is great for fast volume but can't be the sole gold — it asks shallow questions, can drift from the real distribution, and can't support reference-needing Correctness. Pitfalls: (1) questions are mostly “copy-able straight from the doc”, missing real hard cases; (2) the distribution skews to doc-dense areas while real high-frequency phrasings are missed; (3) without human-checked references Correctness is unusable, and noise in auto questions makes the gate “misfire”. To make it trustworthy: treat auto-generation as a draft pool, have humans select + rewrite + label a high-value subset, and mix in real production questions (thumbs-down / handed-off chats) for the true long tail; the CI gate runs reference-free faithfulness/relevancy over the full draft and Correctness over the human subset. How to check the gold itself is good: it should discriminate known good vs bad configs (good scores clearly higher); if it can't, the questions lack discriminative power and need more curation.
🎯 3. 评估是 LLM-as-judge，搬进 CI 后同一个 PR 重跑两次分数会抖，构建一会儿红一会儿绿（flaky）。这种“闸不稳定”你怎么定位和治理？还要不要把它当硬性合并条件？Evaluation is LLM-as-judge; in CI the same PR re-run twice gives jittery scores and a flaky red/green build. How do you diagnose and tame this instability — and should it still be a hard merge requirement?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：抖动来自 judge 的随机性和小样本噪声；靠“降随机 + 增样本 + 留容忍带 + 看趋势”治理，硬闸只卡明显回退、细微抖动转为告警。① 降随机：judge 用 temperature=0、固定模型版本与评判 prompt、二值 rubric，减少不确定性；② 增样本：题太少则单题翻转就让通过率大跳，扩大回归集让比例稳定；③ 容忍带：阈值不卡“等于基线”，而是“低于基线一个明显幅度”才 fail，给噪声留缓冲；④ 分层：把昂贵/不稳的 Correctness 放夜间离线跑，CI 硬闸只用稳定、免参考的忠实/相关；⑤ 看趋势：连续多次低于阈值才阻断，单点抖动只告警。验证治理是否见效：固定一个不动的 PR 重跑 N 次，统计通过率方差，方差落进容忍带以内才算稳。🔑 Key: jitter comes from judge randomness and small-sample noise; tame it with “less randomness + more samples + a tolerance band + trend-watching”, and let the hard gate fire only on clear regressions while small jitter becomes a warning. (1) Less randomness: run the judge at temperature=0, pin the model version and judging prompt, use a binary rubric; (2) more samples: with too few questions one flip swings the pass-rate, so enlarge the regression set to stabilize the ratio; (3) tolerance band: gate on “clearly below baseline”, not “equal to baseline”, leaving room for noise; (4) tiering: run the costly/unstable Correctness offline nightly and keep only stable, reference-free faithfulness/relevancy as the hard CI gate; (5) trend: block only after several consecutive sub-threshold runs, warn on a single dip. Verify the fix by re-running one unchanged PR N times and measuring pass-rate variance — stable once it falls within the tolerance band.
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 你只有 200 条无标准答案的历史问答，想搭一个最小可用的回归评估闸，你会怎么做？（提示：哪几把尺子不需要参考答案？）You have 200 historical Q&A pairs with no reference answers and want a minimal usable regression gate. How would you build it? (Hint: which rulers need no reference?)
第六部分 · 生产进阶

23 · 可观测与追踪

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

一次生产 RAG 查询要走检索 → rerank → LLM 合成好几步，但你通常只看到最后那句答案——答错、答慢、答贵时，根本分不清是哪一步出的问题。可观测（observability）/ 追踪（tracing）把每一步的耗时 / token / 检索到的 node / 成本都记录下来，把黑盒变成一条逐步可见的时间线。LlamaIndex 几乎零成本就能接上：一行 set_global_handler('arize_phoenix') 接到追踪后端，或用零依赖的 LlamaDebugHandler 在本地直接看内部。一句话：把“靠猜”换成“看 trace”。A production RAG query runs several steps — retrieve → rerank → LLM synthesis — yet you usually see only the final answer; when it's wrong, slow, or expensive you can't tell which step is to blame. Observability / tracing records every step's latency / tokens / retrieved nodes / cost, turning a black box into a step-by-step timeline. LlamaIndex makes this nearly free: one line of set_global_handler('arize_phoenix') wires a tracing backend, or the zero-dependency LlamaDebugHandler shows the internals locally. In a line: replace “guessing” with “reading the trace”.

一次 queryOne query

→

🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
像查快递物流：没有单号追踪，你只知道“包裹还没到”（答案不对 / 很慢），却不知卡在哪个环节；接上物流轨迹后，每个中转站的到达时间一目了然，立刻看出是分拣慢了还是派送堵了——trace 之于 RAG，就是物流轨迹之于包裹。
Like tracking a parcel: with no tracking number you only know “it hasn't arrived” (the answer is wrong or slow) but not where it's stuck; turn on the shipping trace and every hub's arrival time is laid bare, so you instantly see whether sorting was slow or delivery was jammed — a trace is to a RAG query what shipment tracking is to a parcel.
trace 里的信号Signal in the trace
这一步暴露什么What it exposes
帮你定位什么问题Which problem it pinpoints
检索到的 nodeRetrieved nodes
实际召回了哪些块、相似度分、命中没命中which chunks came back, similarity scores, hit or miss
答案没依据 → 多半是检索错（块没召到 / 召错）answer ungrounded → usually a retrieval miss (wrong/missing chunk)

retrieve · rerank · LLM 每段各花多少毫秒ms spent in retrieve · rerank · LLM each
慢在哪一步 → 该优化检索、精排还是生成where it's slow → optimize retrieval, rerank or generation

prompt / completion 各多少 token、折算单价prompt / completion token counts and the cost they convert to

trace 里最该看的三类信号：检索到的 node 看“答得对不对”，各步耗时看“慢在哪”，token / 成本看“贵在哪”The three signals worth reading in a trace: retrieved nodes for “is it right”, per-step latency for “where it's slow”, tokens/cost for “where it's pricey”

RAG 多步、中间结果隐藏：可观测是生产调试的地基RAG is multi-step with hidden intermediates: observability is the bedrock of production debugging

RAG 的答案是一条多步流水线跑出来的：查询改写 → 检索 → rerank → 组 prompt → LLM 合成，每一步都可能出错，而你默认只看到最后那句话。答案不对，可能是检索没召到对的块，也可能是块召到了但 LLM 没用好；答案太慢，可能慢在 rerank 的交叉编码器，也可能慢在 LLM 生成；账单太贵，可能是 context 塞太长、也可能是输出太啰嗦。不打开中间结果，这些都只能靠猜——而猜的代价是一版版乱改、还可能“修好一个、碰坏一批”。可观测就是把这条隐藏流水线摊开成数据：每一步记一个 span，带上检索到的 node、相似度、各步耗时、prompt / completion 的 token 与成本。有了它，调试从“凭直觉试”变成“看着证据改”——先定位是检索还是生成的问题，再对症下药。这就是为什么生产 RAG 上线前，可观测往往是要第一个补齐的地基：没有它，后面的评估、调优、降本都是盲飞。
A RAG answer comes out of a multi-step pipeline: query rewrite → retrieve → rerank → build prompt → LLM synthesis, and every step can go wrong while you see only the final sentence by default. A wrong answer might be retrieval missing the right chunk, or the chunk being retrieved but the LLM using it poorly; a slow answer might be slow in the rerank cross-encoder or in LLM generation; an expensive bill might be an over-long context or an over-verbose output. Without opening the intermediates, all of this is guesswork — and guessing costs you version-after-version flailing, with a real risk of “fix one, break many”. Observability lays this hidden pipeline out as data: each step emits a span carrying the retrieved nodes, similarity scores, per-step latency, and prompt / completion tokens and cost. With it, debugging shifts from “try on a hunch” to “change on evidence” — first pinpoint whether it's a retrieval or a generation problem, then treat the right one. That's why, before a production RAG ships, observability is usually the first foundation to put in place: without it, the later evaluation, tuning and cost work is all flying blind.
没有 trace（黑盒、靠猜）No trace (black box, guessing)
用户问“退款多久到账？”答错了。你看不到内部：检索到的是哪几个块？rerank 后留下谁？prompt 里到底塞了什么？只能凭猜改——调 top_k、换 prompt、改 chunk_size，改一版试一版，像蒙着眼修车，可能折腾半天问题根本在另一头。
A user asks “how long until my refund arrives?” and the answer is wrong. You can't see inside: which chunks were retrieved? what survived rerank? what actually went into the prompt? You can only guess — bump top_k, swap the prompt, change chunk_size, one version at a time, like fixing a car blindfolded — and may burn hours while the real cause sits at the other end.
vs
有 trace（每步可见、可定位）With a trace (every step visible)
同一个问题，trace 一摊开：检索这步召回的 5 个 node 里压根没有“退款时效”那条（相似度全偏低）——问题在检索，不在生成。于是直接去补该文档、加 BM25 或调检索，而不是瞎改 prompt；顺带还看到 LLM 这步耗时 1.8s、占了八成延迟，慢在哪也一并清楚。
Same question, trace laid open: the 5 nodes from the retrieval step don't even contain the “refund timing” clause (all low similarity) — the problem is retrieval, not generation. So you go fix that document, add BM25 or tune retrieval instead of randomly editing the prompt; you also notice the LLM step took 1.8s, ~80% of the latency, so where it's slow is clear too.
同一次答错：没有 trace 只能蒙着眼乱改；有 trace 一眼看出是检索没召到、还顺带定位了延迟大头Same wrong answer: without a trace you tweak blindfolded; with a trace you see at a glance it was a retrieval miss — and spot the latency hog too
检索Retrieve200ms · 9%
精排 RerankRerank220ms · 10%
组 promptBuild prompt30ms · 1%
LLM 生成LLM generate1800ms · 80%
一条 trace 的耗时分解：LLM 生成占了约八成——先优化它，别瞎猜One trace's latency split: LLM generation is ~80% — optimize it first, don't guess

把内部接出来：三种常用追踪接法Surfacing the internals: three common ways to trace

怎么接How to plug inCallbackManager 手动挂attach via CallbackManagerset_global_handler('arize_phoenix') 一行one line: set_global_handler('arize_phoenix')set_global_handler('langfuse') 一行one line: set_global_handler('langfuse')

🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
callbacks/global_handlers.py · set_global_handler — 一行切换全局追踪后端（Phoenix / Langfuse 等都走它），core 内置one line to switch the global tracing backend (Phoenix / Langfuse all go through it), built into core
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
llama-index-callbacks-arize-phoenix · arize_phoenix — 把 trace 接到 Arize Phoenix 可视化的集成包（独立安装）the integration package that wires traces into the Arize Phoenix UI (installed separately)
深入：一行接 Phoenix、instrumentation 事件 / span 与后端取舍Deep dive: one-line Phoenix, instrumentation events/spans, and backend trade-offs点击展开expand
🧪 示例：一行接上 Phoenix 看 trace🧪 Example: one line to trace into Phoenix
本地 pip install llama-index-callbacks-arize-phoenix 并启动 Phoenix（px.launch_app() 或独立进程），然后 set_global_handler('arize_phoenix') 一行接上。之后任意 query 无需改代码都会被记录：浏览器里能看到一条 query 的 span 时间线——检索召回了哪些 node、rerank 留下谁、LLM 这步多少 token / 耗时 / 成本，逐层点开。
Locally pip install llama-index-callbacks-arize-phoenix and start Phoenix (px.launch_app() or a standalone process), then one line: set_global_handler('arize_phoenix'). After that any query records itself with no code changes: in the browser you get a span timeline for a query — which nodes retrieval returned, what rerank kept, and the LLM step's tokens / latency / cost, expandable layer by layer.
❓ 为什么生产 RAG 必须可观测❓ Why production RAG must be observable
因为 RAG 是多步且中间结果默认隐藏：你只拿到最后一句答案，却看不到检索召回了什么、各步花了多久、烧了多少 token。答错时，分不清是检索没召到还是生成没用好，只能一版版瞎改、还可能“修一个坏一批”。可观测把每步摊成证据，让调试、评估、降本都有据可依——它是其他生产能力（评估闸、成本优化、告警）的地基，没有它后面全是盲飞。
Because RAG is multi-step with intermediates hidden by default: you get only the final sentence, not what retrieval returned, how long each step took, or how many tokens it burned. On a wrong answer you can't tell a retrieval miss from poor generation, so you flail version by version and risk “fix one, break many”. Observability turns each step into evidence, giving debugging, evaluation and cost work something to stand on — it's the foundation under other production capabilities (eval gates, cost tuning, alerting); without it the rest is flying blind.
⚙️ 内部怎么跑：事件 / span 与 CallbackManager⚙️ How it runs inside: events / spans and the CallbackManager
LlamaIndex 在每个关键环节（检索、rerank、LLM、embedding、合成）发出成对的事件：CBEventType 的 start / end 各一条，配对起来就是一个 span，带上耗时与 payload（检索到的 node、prompt、token 等）。这些事件由挂在 Settings.callback_manager 上的各个 handler 接收：LlamaDebugHandler 把它们打印 / 存成 event pairs，Phoenix / Langfuse 的 handler 则把同样的 span 转成 OpenTelemetry 上报后端。新版还有更细的 instrumentation（dispatcher + span / event）体系，但对使用者而言核心不变：一处挂 handler，全链路自动埋点。
At each key stage (retrieve, rerank, LLM, embedding, synthesis) LlamaIndex emits paired events: a start and an end of a CBEventType that pair into one span carrying duration and a payload (retrieved nodes, prompt, tokens, etc.). These events are received by the handlers attached to Settings.callback_manager: LlamaDebugHandler prints/stores them as event pairs, while the Phoenix / Langfuse handlers turn the same spans into OpenTelemetry sent to a backend. Newer versions add a finer instrumentation system (a dispatcher + spans/events), but for users the core is unchanged: attach a handler in one place and the whole chain is auto-instrumented.
🔀 后端取舍：Phoenix vs Langfuse vs 纯 OTel🔀 Backend trade-offs: Phoenix vs Langfuse vs raw OTel
三条常见路：Arize Phoenix——本地一行起步、可视化强，最适合开发期排查检索 / 延迟，但默认偏单机、非长期留存；Langfuse——可自托管或托管，带团队留存、数据集、标注、线上监控，适合生产长期回放与协作；纯 OpenTelemetry——不绑某个 UI，直接把 span 上报到你已有的可观测栈（Jaeger / Grafana / Datadog 等），最适合已有 OTel 基建、要把 LLM trace 和服务 trace 拼在一起的团队。按开发期 vs 线上、是否要长期留存、是否已有 OTel 栈三点来选。
Three common paths: Arize Phoenix — one-line local start, strong visualization, best for dev-time triage of retrieval / latency, but defaults to single-machine and isn't for long-term retention; Langfuse — self-hosted or hosted, with team retention, datasets, annotations and production monitoring, suited to production replay and collaboration; raw OpenTelemetry — not tied to one UI, exporting spans straight into your existing observability stack (Jaeger / Grafana / Datadog), best for teams that already run OTel and want LLM traces stitched together with service traces. Choose along three axes: dev vs production, long-term retention or not, and whether you already run OTel.
一行接入：set_global_handler('arize_phoenix') 之后，任意 query 自动记录到 PhoenixOne line: after set_global_handler('arize_phoenix'), any query auto-records into Phoenix
from llama_index.core import set_global_handler

# 一行接入追踪后端（需 pip install llama-index-callbacks-arize-phoenix 并本地启动 Phoenix）
set_global_handler('arize_phoenix')

# 之后任意 query 都会被记录：检索到的 node、各步耗时、token、成本
index.as_query_engine().query('退款多久到账？')
零依赖看内部：LlamaDebugHandler + CallbackManager 打印每个事件对的耗时与中间结果Zero-dep internals: LlamaDebugHandler + CallbackManager prints each event pair's latency and intermediate results
from llama_index.core import Settings
from llama_index.core.callbacks import CallbackManager, LlamaDebugHandler

# 本地零依赖看内部：每个事件的耗时与中间结果
debug = LlamaDebugHandler(print_trace_on_end=True)
Settings.callback_manager = CallbackManager([debug])

index.as_query_engine().query('保修期多久？')
print(debug.get_event_pairs())   # 取检索/LLM 等事件对，看各步耗时
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • RAG 是多步、中间结果隐藏的流水线：可观测把检索 · rerank · LLM 每步的耗时 / token / node / 成本摊成证据。RAG is a multi-step pipeline with hidden intermediates: observability lays each step's (retrieve · rerank · LLM) latency / tokens / nodes / cost out as evidence.
  • 答错先看 trace：检索到的 node 对不对——分清是检索没召到还是生成没用好，再对症下药。On a wrong answer, read the trace first: are the retrieved nodes right — separate a retrieval miss from poor generation, then treat the right one.
  • 一行接入：set_global_handler('arize_phoenix') 接可视化后端；零依赖用 LlamaDebugHandler + CallbackManager 本地看事件对。Plug in with one line: set_global_handler('arize_phoenix') for a visual backend; zero-dep, use LlamaDebugHandler + CallbackManager to read event pairs locally.
  • 后端按场景选：Phoenix 开发期可视化、Langfuse 线上长期留存、纯 OTel 并入已有可观测栈。Pick the backend by use: Phoenix for dev-time visualization, Langfuse for long-term production retention, raw OTel to merge into an existing observability stack.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
可观测的精髓是把 RAG 这条隐藏的多步流水线变成可读的证据：每步一个带 耗时 / token / node 的 span，让调试从“凭感觉一版版试”升级成“看着 trace 定位是哪一步”——它是评估、调优、降本一切生产能力的地基。
The essence of observability is turning RAG's hidden multi-step pipeline into readable evidence: one span per step with latency / tokens / nodes, upgrading debugging from “try version after version on feel” to “read the trace and pinpoint the step” — the foundation beneath evaluation, tuning and cost work, every production capability.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. 线上一条问答答错了，你打开它的 trace。最该先看哪一项来判断“是检索还是生成的问题”？A production answer is wrong and you open its trace. What should you look at first to decide “retrieval problem or generation problem”?
  1. LLM 这步花了多少毫秒how many ms the LLM step took
  2. 检索到的 node 里有没有正确依据、相似度高不高whether the retrieved nodes contain the right evidence and their similarity
  3. 这次请求一共烧了多少钱the total cost of this request
  4. 用的是哪个 embedding 模型which embedding model was used
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：BAnswer: B 先看检索召回的 node：若正确依据压根没召到，那是检索问题（调 chunk / 加 BM25 / 调 top_k），改 prompt 没用；只有在“召到了却答错”时才是生成问题。耗时和成本是性能 / 费用维度，不用来判断答案对错的归因。Read the retrieved nodes first: if the right evidence was never recalled, it's a retrieval problem (tune chunking / add BM25 / adjust top_k) and editing the prompt won't help; only when it “was recalled yet still wrong” is it a generation problem. Latency and cost are performance / spend axes, not for attributing correctness.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 线上反馈“某些问答特别慢，要等好几秒”。你怎么用 trace 定位慢在检索、rerank 还是 LLM？定位到之后又分别怎么治？你怎么验证真的快了、而不是把准确率换走了？Production reports “some Q&A is very slow, several seconds”. How do you use a trace to localize whether it's slow in retrieval, rerank or the LLM? Once localized, how do you treat each — and how do you verify it actually got faster without trading away accuracy?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：先用 trace 把端到端延迟按 span 拆开，看每步各占多少毫秒，找到耗时大头那一步再对症治，最后用“延迟分位 + 质量分数”一起验证别只换不赚。① 定位：打开慢请求的 span 时间线——若检索占大头，多半是向量库慢 / top_k 过大 / 索引没建好；若 rerank 占大头，是交叉编码器在大候选集上太慢；若 LLM 占大头（最常见），看 prompt 是不是太长、输出是不是太啰嗦。② 对症：检索慢 → 建索引 / 降 top_k / 换更快的库；rerank 慢 → 先缩小候选集再精排、或换更轻的 reranker；LLM 慢 → 压缩 context、限制 max_tokens、必要时换更快模型或上流式。③ 验证：固定一组真实查询，比较改前后的 p50 / p95 延迟，同时跑评估确认忠实度 / 命中率没有下降——只有“更快且不更差”才算数。🔑 Key: use the trace to split end-to-end latency by span, see how many ms each step costs, fix the biggest hog first, then verify with “latency percentiles + quality scores” so you don't trade speed for accuracy. (1) Localize: open the slow request's span timeline — if retrieval dominates, it's usually a slow vector store / too-large top_k / a missing index; if rerank dominates, the cross-encoder is slow over a big candidate set; if the LLM dominates (most common), check whether the prompt is too long or the output too verbose. (2) Treat: slow retrieval → build an index / lower top_k / a faster store; slow rerank → shrink the candidate set before reranking or use a lighter reranker; slow LLM → compress context, cap max_tokens, switch to a faster model or stream. (3) Verify: on a fixed set of real queries compare p50 / p95 latency before/after while running evals to confirm faithfulness / hit-rate didn't drop — only “faster and no worse” counts.

→

→
