图谱查询四步：找种子 → 顺边多跳 → 带回原文 → 综合；“顺边多跳”这一步正是向量做不到的Graph query in four steps: seed → multi-hop walk → attach text → synthesize; the “multi-hop walk” is exactly what vectors can't do
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
indices/property_graph/sub_retrievers/ · LLMSynonymRetriever · VectorContextRetriever — 默认两路子检索器：同义词扩展找种子节点 + 向量上下文召回相邻文本，再顺边多跳。the two default sub-retrievers: synonym expansion seeds nodes + vector context pulls neighboring text, then traversal hops along edges.

何时用图、何时用向量When a graph, when vectors

不是所有 RAG 都该上图谱，判断只看一件事：问题靠不靠“关系”。当知识本身是一张关系网（产品-配件-兼容、人物-公司-职位、论文-引用），问题又要多跳推理（A 的 B 的 C），图谱的“顺边遍历”几乎是唯一能答全的方式。反过来，如果问题只是找一段语义相近的话（“退款政策怎么写的”），或关系稀疏、一跳就够，那纯向量更便宜、更快、够用，花 LLM 抽一整张图并不划算。实务里两者常互补：向量管“找到相关段落”，图谱管“把相关事实连起来”，按问题类型路由（回想 L18 的 Router）。
Not every RAG needs a graph; the test is one thing: does the question hinge on “relations”. When the knowledge is itself a web of relations (product-part-compatibility, person-company-role, paper-citation) and the question needs multi-hop reasoning (A's B's C), a graph's edge traversal is almost the only way to answer it fully. Conversely, if the question just finds a semantically close passage (“what does the refund policy say”) or relations are sparse and one hop suffices, plain vectors are cheaper, faster, and enough — paying an LLM to extract a whole graph isn't worth it. In practice the two often complement: vectors “find the relevant passage”, a graph “connects the relevant facts”, routed by question type (recall L18's Router).
对比项Aspect图谱 RAGGraph RAG向量 RAGVector RAG
召回的是Recalls连起来的事实（实体-关系-实体）connected facts (entity-relation-entity)相似的片段（top-k 近邻）similar chunks (top-k neighbors)
最擅长Best at多跳 / 关系密集问答multi-hop / relation-dense Q&A语义相似 / 换种问法semantic similarity / rephrasings
构建成本Build cost高：LLM 逐文档抽三元组high: LLM extracts triples per doc低：切块 + embeddinglow: chunk + embedding
盲区Blind spot关系稀疏时性价比低poor ROI when relations are sparse跨片段的关系会丢loses cross-chunk relations
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
纯向量检索像在一摞书里翻找长得像的书页：哪一页和你手里的纸看起来最像就抽出来——换种说法也能找到，但它不知道页与页之间的关系。图谱像顺着引用链一页页翻下去：从这一页的脚注找到它引用的那一页，再顺着那一页的引用接着翻，把一条线索串起来的内容都找齐——这正是多跳问题需要的。
Pure vector search is like thumbing through a stack for the page that looks alike: pull out whichever page looks most like the sheet in your hand — rephrasings still match, but it knows nothing about how pages relate. A graph is like following a citation chain page by page: from this page's footnote you reach the page it cites, then follow that page's citations onward, collecting everything strung along one thread — exactly what a multi-hop question needs.
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 向量召回“相似片段”，图谱召回“连起来的事实”；多跳关系（A→B→C）纯向量答不出。Vectors recall “similar chunks”, a graph recalls “connected facts”; multi-hop relations (A→B→C) are beyond pure vectors.
  • 用 PropertyGraphIndex.from_documents(kg_extractors=[...]) 建图；SchemaLLMPathExtractor 用 schema 约束 LLM 抽出的实体/关系，图更干净。Build with PropertyGraphIndex.from_documents(kg_extractors=[...]); SchemaLLMPathExtractor constrains the LLM's entities/relations to a schema for a cleaner graph.
  • 查询默认两路子检索器：LLMSynonymRetriever（同义词扩展找种子）+ VectorContextRetriever（向量上下文），再顺边多跳；include_text=True 带回原文。Querying uses two default sub-retrievers: LLMSynonymRetriever (synonym seeds) + VectorContextRetriever (vector context), then multi-hop traversal; include_text=True brings back source text.
  • 关系密集 / 多跳问答用图谱，普通相似检索用向量；图的代价是抽取贵、构建慢。Relation-dense / multi-hop Q&A → graph, ordinary similarity → vectors; a graph's cost is pricey extraction, slow build.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
图谱 RAG 的精髓，是把检索的问题从“哪段话最像”换成“哪些事实连得上”。向量把文档压成一堆互不相连的点，只能按距离取近邻；图谱先用 LLM 把文档还原成实体与关系的网，于是“A 的供应商的总部在哪国”这种跨多跳的问题，能顺着边一步步走到答案——这是纯相似度结构上做不到的。代价也很实在：抽取要烧 LLM、建库更慢，图的质量取决于抽取的质量。所以工程判断不是“图谱更高级所以要上”，而是“我的问题到底靠不靠多跳关系”：靠，就为那张图付抽取的钱；不靠，向量又快又省，别为用不上的关系买单。
The essence of Graph RAG is turning retrieval's question from “which passage looks most alike” into “which facts can be connected”. Vectors squash documents into a cloud of unconnected points and can only take nearest neighbors by distance; a graph first has an LLM reconstruct documents into a web of entities and relations, so a multi-hop question like “which country is the HQ of A's supplier in” can be walked edge by edge to the answer — something pure similarity structurally cannot do. The cost is real: extraction burns LLM calls and indexing is slower, and graph quality rides on extraction quality. So the engineering call isn't “a graph is fancier, so use it” but “does my question actually hinge on multi-hop relations”: if it does, pay the extraction price for that graph; if it doesn't, vectors are fast and cheap — don't pay for relations you'll never traverse.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. 下列哪种问题最该用图谱 RAG 而非纯向量？Which question most warrants Graph RAG over pure vectors?
  1. 找与“退款政策”语义相近的段落find passages semantically close to “refund policy”
  2. 把文档翻译成英文translate the document into English
  3. X 的供应商的总部在哪个国家（多跳）which country is the HQ of X's supplier in (multi-hop)
  4. 这段话的情感是正还是负is this passage's sentiment positive or negative
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：CAnswer: C 正确的是“多跳关系查询”（X 的供应商的总部在哪个国家）：要顺着 供应商→总部→国家 的边走，图谱把事实存成可遍历的三元组正好胜任。找语义相近段落是相似检索（向量更划算），判断情感正负是分类，翻译就是翻译——都用不上图的多跳能力。The correct one is the “multi-hop relation query” (which country is X's supplier's HQ in): you must walk supplier→HQ→country, and a graph stores facts as traversable triples for exactly this. Finding semantically close passages is similarity retrieval (vectors are cheaper), judging sentiment is classification, and translation is translation — none need a graph's multi-hop power.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 图谱 RAG 里，抽取器（extractor）质量差会怎样？你会怎么控住抽取质量、又怎么验证它够好？In Graph RAG, what happens when the extractor quality is poor? How would you keep it under control and verify it's good enough?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：图的质量 = 抽取的质量——抽错 / 抽漏会造出错误的边，多跳时一路放大成错答；靠 ① schema 约束、② 评估抽取准确率、③ 人工校验高价值实体 三道闸控住。① 用 SchemaLLMPathExtractor 上 schema：预先声明允许的实体 / 关系类型，把 LLM 关进栏里，不让它乱造关系（“幻觉边”）；② 评估抽取准确率：抽样三元组和人工标注的金标比 precision / recall，差就换更强的抽取 LLM 或细化 schema；③ 人工校验高价值实体：被很多跳路过的枢纽实体（核心产品、关键厂商）一旦错，下游全错，优先人工过一遍；④ 端到端验证：用一组多跳问答金标，看修抽取前后答案对不对——别只盯抽取本身，要落到下游答案质量。🔑 Key: graph quality = extraction quality — wrong/missing extractions create bad edges that multi-hop then amplifies into wrong answers; control it with three gates: (1) schema constraints, (2) measuring extraction accuracy, (3) human-verifying high-value entities. (1) Add a schema via SchemaLLMPathExtractor: declare the allowed entity/relation types up front to cage the LLM so it can't invent stray relations (“hallucinated edges”); (2) measure extraction accuracy: sample triples against a human-labeled gold set for precision/recall, and if low, swap in a stronger extraction LLM or refine the schema; (3) human-verify high-value entities: hub entities that many hops pass through (core products, key vendors) corrupt everything downstream if wrong, so review them first; (4) end-to-end check: use a set of multi-hop QA gold questions and compare answer correctness before/after — don't just stare at extraction, tie it back to downstream answer quality.
🎯 2. 什么时候你会不上图谱、继续用纯向量？你拿什么数据支撑这个决定？When would you not adopt a graph and stick with pure vectors? What data backs that call?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：关系稀疏、一跳就够、或构建 / 维护成本扛不住时，纯向量更划算——别为用不上的关系付抽取的钱。① 关系稀疏：语料就是一篇篇独立文档、没什么实体间链接，建图抽不出几条有用的边；② 一跳就够：问题大多是“找一段相关的话 / 查单个事实”，向量的相似召回已经够好；③ 成本扛不住：图要 LLM 逐文档抽三元组，建库慢且贵，语料还频繁更新就要反复重抽，延迟 / 预算紧时不划算。怎么用数据：统计真实查询里真正多跳 / 关系型的占比——若很低，就只把这一小撮路由到图谱（混合），其余留给向量；再对比“向量 vs 图谱”在这批问题上的命中率 / 答案质量增量，是否抵得过多出的成本与延迟。🔑 Key: when relations are sparse, one hop suffices, or build/maintenance cost is too high, plain vectors win — don't pay extraction cost for relations you'll never traverse. (1) Sparse relations: the corpus is independent documents with few entity links, so building a graph extracts few useful edges; (2) one hop is enough: most questions are “find a relevant passage / look up a single fact”, where vector similarity already does well; (3) cost is too high: a graph needs an LLM to extract triples per document — slow and pricey to build, and a frequently-changing corpus forces repeated re-extraction; not worth it under tight latency/budget. How to use data: measure the share of real queries that are genuinely multi-hop / relational — if it's low, route only that minority to a graph (hybrid) and keep the rest on vectors; then compare “vector vs graph” hit-rate / answer-quality lift on that subset against the extra cost and latency.
🎯 3. 为什么用新的 PropertyGraphIndex 而不是旧的 KnowledgeGraphIndex？在关系表达 / 构建成本 / 可解释性上，它和纯向量又各自怎么取舍？Why use the newer PropertyGraphIndex instead of the legacy KnowledgeGraphIndex? And how do the two trade off against pure vectors on relation modeling / build cost / explainability?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：PropertyGraphIndex 是新一代图谱抽象，实体 / 关系能带属性与类型、可挂多路子检索器、可上 schema 约束，表达力和可控性都强过只存裸三元组的旧 KnowledgeGraphIndex；和纯向量比，图用“可解释的多跳路径”换“更高的构建成本”。选型沿一条轴：关系越重、越需要可解释，越往图谱走。PropertyGraph 表达最丰富、可解释性最好（能看到走了哪条边），但抽取要烧 LLM；旧 KnowledgeGraph 只存简单三元组、工具较旧，新项目一般直接上 PropertyGraph；纯向量不建模关系、最便宜最快，但答案只有一个相似分、近乎黑箱。一句话：按“问题靠不靠关系”和“要不要可解释路径”选档。🔑 Key: PropertyGraphIndex is the newer graph abstraction whose entities/relations carry properties and types, plugs in multiple sub-retrievers, and supports schema constraints, so it's more expressive and controllable than the legacy KnowledgeGraphIndex that stores bare triples; versus pure vectors, a graph trades “higher build cost” for an “explainable multi-hop path”. The choice runs along one axis: the more relations matter and the more you need explainability, the more you lean toward a graph. PropertyGraph is the most expressive and explainable (you can see which edges were walked) but its extraction burns LLM calls; the legacy KnowledgeGraph stores only simple triples with older tooling, so new projects usually go straight to PropertyGraph; pure vectors model no relations and are cheapest/fastest but give only a similarity score, nearly a black box. In a line: pick the tier by “does the question hinge on relations” and “do you need an explainable path”.

💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 你的知识库是产品-配件-兼容关系网，为什么图谱比向量更合适？（提示：关系 / 多跳 / 可解释路径）Your knowledge base is a product-part-compatibility web of relations. Why is a graph more suitable than vectors? (Hint: relations / multi-hop / explainable path)
第七部分 · 超越文本 RAG

28 · 结构化数据查询

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

到这里，检索一直在做同一件事——“找相似”：把问题和文档变成向量、取回最像的片段。可一旦问题是“上个月各区域的总销售额、降序排列”这种要精确算数字的，向量就无能为力：答案不在某一段话里现成写着，而要把成千上万行逐笔加总、按区域分组、再排序。这一课换一种思路：别让向量算账，把结构化数据交给天生会精确计算的工具——用 text-to-SQL 让数据库算、用 PandasQueryEngine 让内存表算；同时盯紧一个绕不开的代价：这些引擎在执行 LLM 生成的代码。Up to here retrieval kept doing one thing — “find similar”: turn the question and docs into vectors and fetch the most alike chunks. But the moment the question is something like “total sales per region last month, sorted descending” that needs an exact number, vectors are helpless: the answer isn't sitting ready in any passage — it requires summing row by row, grouping by region and then sorting thousands of rows. This lesson flips the approach: don't make vectors do the accounting; hand structured data to tools born to compute exactly — use text-to-SQL so the database computes, and PandasQueryEngine so an in-memory table computes — all while watching one unavoidable cost: these engines execute LLM-generated code.

痛点：数字、聚合、精确筛选，塞进向量必然不准The pain: numbers, aggregation, exact filtering — forced into vectors, bound to be wrong

向量检索的本事是“找像的”：把每段文字编码成语义向量，召回和问题最相似的 top-k 片段。这对“讲了什么”的非结构化文字很灵，碰到“算出确切数字”却立刻露馅。问“上个月每个区域的总销售额、降序排列”，答案不是哪段话里写好的句子，而要把成千上万行订单加总、分组、排序——向量既不会做加法，也保证不了“全”：top-k 只取几片，漏一行结果就错。把订单表、财务报表、监控指标这种结构化数据硬编码成 embedding，等于让一个擅长“模糊联想”的系统去做“精确算账”，结果必然是“看起来差不多、其实算错”。这类问题的正解只有一个方向：别让向量算，把精确计算交给本来就为它而生的工具——数据库与 DataFrame。
Vector search is good at “finding the alike”: encode each passage into a semantic vector and recall the top-k chunks most similar to the question. That shines on unstructured text about “what was said”, but it falls apart the instant you need an exact number. Ask “total sales per region last month, sorted descending” and the answer isn't a ready-made sentence in some passage — it requires totalling, grouping and sorting thousands of rows of orders. Vectors can't do arithmetic and can't guarantee completeness: top-k takes a few chunks, and miss one row and the result is wrong. Hard-coding an orders table, a financial report or a monitoring metric into embeddings asks a system built for “fuzzy association” to do “exact accounting” — the result is bound to “look about right but compute wrong”. There's only one right direction: don't make vectors compute; hand exact calculation to the tools born for it — databases and DataFrames.
向量检索Vector
问“各区域总销售额”，只捞回几段看起来相关的文字，数字还得你自己凑——漏行、算错
ask “total sales per region” and it just pulls a few seems-related snippets; you still patch the numbers yourself — missed rows, wrong totals
vs
text-to-SQLtext-to-SQL
LLM 写 GROUP BY · SUM · ORDER BY，数据库逐行精确算，结果又全又准
the LLM writes GROUP BY · SUM · ORDER BY; the database computes exactly, row by row — complete and correct
同一个数字问题：向量只会“找相似”，text-to-SQL 才能“精确算”Same numeric question: vectors only “find similar”, text-to-SQL actually “computes exactly”

text-to-SQL：LLM 写 SQL，数据库做精确计算text-to-SQL: the LLM writes SQL, the database does the exact compute

数据库天生就会“精确算账”：GROUP BY 分组、SUM 求和、ORDER BY 排序，几十年的引擎优化保证又快又准。text-to-SQL 的思路就是分工：把表结构（schema）喂给 LLM，让它据此写出 SQL，交数据库执行，再把结果用自然语言讲回来——LLM 只做“把人话翻成 SQL”这件它擅长的事，真正的计算落在数据库上。SQLDatabase 包住数据库连接（include_tables 限定可见表），NLSQLTableQueryEngine 把“自然语言 → SQL → 执行 → 答案”串成一个查询引擎。
A database is born to do “exact accounting”: GROUP BY to group, SUM to total, ORDER BY to sort — decades of engine optimization make it fast and correct. text-to-SQL is just a division of labor: feed the schema to the LLM, have it write SQL from that, hand it to the database to execute, then phrase the result back in natural language — the LLM only does the one thing it's good at, “translate human words into SQL”, while the real computation lands on the database. SQLDatabase wraps the connection (include_tables limits the visible tables) and NLSQLTableQueryEngine chains “NL → SQL → execute → answer” into one query engine.
可 schema 一大就有新麻烦：库里有几百张表时，把所有表结构塞进提示词既超长又贵，还会让 LLM 在无关表里挑花眼、写错 SQL。解法是先选表、再写 SQL：把每张表的描述做成对象、建一个 ObjectIndex，查询时先检索出与问题最相关的少数几张表，只把这几张的 schema 交给 LLM。承担这一步的是 SQLTableRetrieverQueryEngine——它比 NLSQLTableQueryEngine 多了“先按问题召回相关表”的检索器，正是为大库设计：提示词短了，选错表、串错列的概率自然降下来。
But a big schema brings a new problem: with hundreds of tables, stuffing every schema into the prompt is huge and expensive and tempts the LLM to pick the wrong table and write wrong SQL. The fix is select tables first, then write SQL: turn each table's description into an object and build an ObjectIndex; at query time first retrieve the few tables most relevant to the question and give only those schemas to the LLM. That job falls to SQLTableRetrieverQueryEngine — it adds a “retrieve relevant tables by the question first” retriever on top of NLSQLTableQueryEngine, designed exactly for large databases: a shorter prompt naturally lowers the odds of the wrong table or a crossed-up column.
自然语言进、SQL 出、数据库算：include_tables 限定可见表，把精确计算交给数据库NL in, SQL out, DB computes: include_tables limits the visible tables, hand the exact math to the database
from llama_index.core import SQLDatabase
from llama_index.core.query_engine import NLSQLTableQueryEngine

sql_db = SQLDatabase(engine, include_tables=["orders"])
qe = NLSQLTableQueryEngine(sql_database=sql_db, tables=["orders"])
print(qe.query("上个月每个区域的总销售额是多少，降序排列？"))

text-to-SQL：把精确计算交给数据库，LLM 只负责翻译text-to-SQL: hand exact compute to the DB; the LLM only translates

内存表：交给 PandasQueryEngineIn-memory tables: hand them to PandasQueryEngine

不是所有结构化数据都躺在数据库里。很多时候你手上就是一个 pandas.DataFrame——一份刚读进来的 CSV、一段 API 返回、一张算好的中间表。为这点数据起一个数据库太重，PandasQueryEngine 直接让 LLM 对 DataFrame 干活：把列名和样例给 LLM，让它写一小段 pandas 代码（如 df.groupby(...).sum()），执行后把结果讲回来。“销量最高的 3 个产品”这种小分析，几行就出；verbose=True 还会打印它生成的代码，方便你核对它到底算了什么。它和 text-to-SQL 是同一套思路（LLM 写代码、引擎执行），只是把“数据库 + SQL”换成了“内存表 + pandas”。
Not all structured data lives in a database. Often you just hold a pandas.DataFrame — a freshly read CSV, an API response, a computed intermediate table. Spinning up a database for that is overkill; PandasQueryEngine lets the LLM work the DataFrame directly: give it the column names and a sample, have it write a small snippet of pandas code (e.g. df.groupby(...).sum()), execute it, and phrase the result back. A small analysis like “the top-3 products by sales” comes out in a few lines; verbose=True also prints the generated code so you can check what it actually computed. It's the same idea as text-to-SQL (the LLM writes code, an engine runs it), just swapping “database + SQL” for “in-memory table + pandas”.
内存 DataFrame 直接问：LLM 写 pandas、引擎执行；verbose 打印生成的代码便于核对Ask an in-memory DataFrame directly: the LLM writes pandas, the engine runs it; verbose prints the generated code to check
# pip install llama-index-experimental  —— core 0.14.22 仅留会抛弃用警告的占位实现
from llama_index.experimental.query_engine import PandasQueryEngine

qe = PandasQueryEngine(df=df, verbose=True)   # ⚠️ 会 eval LLM 生成的 Python，仅用于可信环境
print(qe.query("销量最高的 3 个产品是哪些？"))

按数据形态选工具——数字别硬塞向量pick by data shape — don't force numbers into vectors

安全：它们在执行 LLM 生成的代码Safety: they execute LLM-generated code

这两个引擎好用，但有一个必须正视的共同前提：它们都在执行 LLM 生成的代码。PandasQueryEngine 会 eval 一段 LLM 写的 Python，NLSQLTableQueryEngine 会把 LLM 写的 SQL 真的跑在你的数据库上。一旦输入不可信，提示注入就能诱导模型写出 DROP TABLE、DELETE、越权去读别的表，甚至（Pandas 这边）执行任意 Python——这不是“答错了”，是“被人借你的手执行命令”。
These two engines are handy, but they share one premise you must face: both execute LLM-generated code. PandasQueryEngine evals a snippet of LLM-written Python, and NLSQLTableQueryEngine actually runs the LLM's SQL on your database. The moment input is untrusted, prompt injection can coax the model into DROP TABLE, DELETE, reading other tables it shouldn't, or (on the Pandas side) running arbitrary Python — that's not “a wrong answer”, it's “someone executing commands through your hands”.
所以上线前的第一要务不是跑通，而是关进笼子：① 数据库一律用只读、最小权限的账号，能 SELECT 不能写、只看该看的表/视图；② Pandas 这类引擎放进沙箱/隔离进程/容器，限制可用模块与文件系统；③ 只对可信输入开放，别把这种引擎直接怼到匿名用户面前。事实上，llama-index-core 0.14.22 已经把 PandasQueryEngine 做成会抛弃用警告的占位实现，把真正能跑的版本挪到了 llama-index-experimental（from llama_index.experimental.query_engine import PandasQueryEngine），并白纸黑字写明“会任意执行代码、请在安全环境使用”——库本身就用这种“默认不让用”的姿态提醒你：方便和危险是绑在一起的。
So the first priority before shipping isn't getting it to run — it's caging it: (1) give the database a read-only, least-privilege account — SELECT but no writes, only the tables/views it should see; (2) put Pandas-style engines in a sandbox / isolated process / container, restricting modules and filesystem; (3) expose it only to trusted input, never wire such an engine straight to anonymous users. In fact, llama-index-core 0.14.22 already ships PandasQueryEngine as a shim that raises a deprecation warning, moving the runnable version to llama-index-experimental (from llama_index.experimental.query_engine import PandasQueryEngine) and stating in black and white that it “allows arbitrary code execution; use in a secure environment” — the library itself uses this “off by default” stance to remind you that convenience and danger come bound together.
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
向量检索像凭“模糊回忆”找最像的一段话：问“上个月华东区卖了多少”，它只会捞回几段“看起来相关”的文字，真要把数字加起来还得靠你自己、还容易漏。text-to-SQL 像“拿计算器精确算”：让数据库去 GROUP BY · SUM · ORDER BY，算出来的数字又全又准。要数字，就别问“模糊回忆”，去按“计算器”。
Vector search is like fishing by “fuzzy memory” for the passage that looks most alike: ask “how much did the East region sell last month” and it pulls back a few “seems-related” snippets, leaving the actual arithmetic to you — and easy to miss rows. text-to-SQL is like “reaching for a calculator”: let the database GROUP BY · SUM · ORDER BY, and the number comes back complete and correct. When you need a number, don't ask “fuzzy memory” — press the “calculator”.
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 数字 / 聚合 / 精确筛选别塞向量——向量只会“找相似”，算不准 SUM/COUNT/排序；结构化数据交给能精确计算的引擎。Don't force numbers / aggregation / exact filtering into vectors — vectors only “find similar” and can't compute SUM/COUNT/sort; hand structured data to engines that compute exactly.
  • text-to-SQL：让 LLM 据表结构写 SQL、数据库执行（NLSQLTableQueryEngine）；表多时先用 ObjectIndex + SQLTableRetrieverQueryEngine 选相关表再生成 SQL。text-to-SQL: the LLM writes SQL from the schema and the database executes it (NLSQLTableQueryEngine); with many tables, first select relevant tables via ObjectIndex + SQLTableRetrieverQueryEngine, then generate SQL.
  • 内存 DataFrame 用 PandasQueryEngine 做快速表分析（LLM 写 pandas、引擎执行）。For an in-memory DataFrame, use PandasQueryEngine for quick table analysis (the LLM writes pandas, the engine runs it).
  • ⚠️ 安全：Pandas/SQL 引擎都在执行 LLM 生成的代码——必须沙箱 / 只读账号 / 最小权限 / 限可信输入；core 0.14.22 已把 PandasQueryEngine 移到 llama-index-experimental 并要求“安全环境”。⚠️ Safety: Pandas/SQL engines both execute LLM-generated code — you must sandbox / use a read-only account / least privilege / restrict to trusted input; core 0.14.22 has moved PandasQueryEngine to llama-index-experimental and requires a “secure environment”.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
结构化数据查询的精髓，是把“该谁来算”想清楚：向量擅长“找相似”，却天生不会“精确算数字”——SUM、COUNT、GROUP BY、环比这些，硬塞进 embedding 只会得到“看起来差不多”的错答。正确做法是按数据形态选工具：非结构化文档走向量，数据库表走 text-to-SQL，内存表走 Pandas，让数据库 / 解释器去做它最擅长的精确计算，LLM 只负责“把人话翻成查询”。代价也很实在：这些引擎都在执行 LLM 生成的代码，把“翻译”的便利和“任意执行”的风险绑在了一起——所以工程上第一件事不是跑通，而是关进沙箱、换只读账号、收最小权限。一句话：数字别硬塞向量，但给数据库写 SQL 的权力也要锁死。
The essence of structured-data querying is getting “who should do the math” right: vectors are great at “finding similar” but inherently can't “compute exact numbers” — SUM, COUNT, GROUP BY, quarter-over-quarter forced into an embedding only yield a “close-looking” wrong answer. The fix is to pick the tool by data shape: unstructured docs → vectors, database tables → text-to-SQL, in-memory tables → Pandas, letting the database / interpreter do the exact compute it's best at while the LLM only “translates human questions into a query”. The cost is real too: these engines all execute LLM-generated code, binding the convenience of “translation” to the risk of “arbitrary execution” — so the first engineering move isn't getting it to run, it's caging it: sandbox, swap in a read-only account, cut to least privilege. In a line: don't force numbers into vectors, but lock down the power to write SQL against your database too.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. “各区域季度环比增长率”最该用哪种方式？Which approach best fits “quarter-over-quarter growth rate per region”?
  1. 向量检索vector retrieval
  2. text-to-SQLtext-to-SQL
  3. HyDE 查询改写HyDE query rewrite
  4. rerank 重排序rerank
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：BAnswer: B 正确的是 text-to-SQL：季度环比增长率是聚合计算（按季度分组、求和，再算环比），要让 LLM 写出 SQL、交数据库精确算。其余三个都在解决“找相似”而非“精确算数字”——向量检索按语义近似召回片段，rerank 重排序只是把已召回的片段重新排个序，HyDE 查询改写是先造个假设答案再去检索；它们都不会做 GROUP BY/SUM 这类精确聚合。The right one is text-to-SQL: quarter-over-quarter growth is an aggregation (group by quarter, sum, then compute the ratio), so have the LLM write SQL and let the database compute it exactly. The other three all solve “find similar”, not “compute exact numbers” — vector retrieval recalls chunks by semantic proximity, rerank only reorders already-retrieved chunks, and HyDE drafts a hypothetical answer to retrieve with; none of them do GROUP BY/SUM-style exact aggregation.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你的 text-to-SQL 在一个几百张表的库上准确率很低——经常选错表、写错 join。你会怎么系统地把它救回来？Your text-to-SQL has low accuracy on a hundreds-of-tables database — it keeps picking the wrong table and botching joins. How would you systematically rescue it?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：大库的关键不是“让 LLM 更聪明”，而是“先把 schema 缩小”——只把相关的几张表喂给它，再用示例和约束兜底。① 先选表再写 SQL：用 ObjectIndex + SQLTableRetrieverQueryEngine，查询时先按问题检索出最相关的少数表，把上百张表的 schema 压到几张，提示词短了、选错率自然降；② 给好表/列描述：为每张表、关键列写清用途，LLM 才分得清 amount 和 net_amount；③ few-shot 示例：放几条“问题→正确 SQL”的范例，教它本库的 join 习惯与命名；④ 限定可用面：用只读视图把复杂表预先 join、改成业务友好的字段，缩小它能碰的范围；⑤ 评估闭环：建一组“问题→金标结果”，用执行结果是否一致量准确率，针对错例迭代描述与示例。一句话：缩小 schema，比换更大的模型更有效。🔑 Key: the lever for a big database isn't “make the LLM smarter”, it's “shrink the schema first” — feed it only the few relevant tables, then backstop with examples and constraints. (1) Select tables before writing SQL: with ObjectIndex + SQLTableRetrieverQueryEngine, first retrieve the few most relevant tables per question, collapsing hundreds of schemas to a handful — a shorter prompt means fewer wrong picks; (2) good table/column descriptions: document each table and key column so the LLM can tell amount from net_amount; (3) few-shot examples: include a few “question → correct SQL” pairs to teach this DB's join habits and naming; (4) restrict the surface: use read-only views that pre-join complex tables into business-friendly fields, shrinking what it can touch; (5) an eval loop: build “question → gold result” pairs and measure accuracy by whether execution results match, iterating descriptions and examples on the failures. In a line: shrinking the schema beats reaching for a bigger model.

→

🎯 2. 用户的一个问题里既要查文档（“退货政策怎么说的”）又要算数字（“上季度退货率多少”）。你怎么路由，让每部分走对引擎？A single user question needs both a document lookup (“what does the return policy say”) and a number (“what was last quarter's return rate”). How do you route so each part hits the right engine?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：用 RouterQueryEngine 按“问题类型”分流——找文字走向量、算数字走 SQL；一个问题同时要两类时再拆成子问题各查各的、最后合并（呼应 L18 的路由、L30 的查询分解）。① 路由：给 Router 挂两个工具——“文档向量引擎”和“text-to-SQL 引擎”，各写清能力描述（“擅长政策/条款类语义问答” vs “擅长订单/指标的精确统计”），由 LLM 选择器按问题选；② 拆分：用 SubQuestionQueryEngine 把复合问题拆成“政策是什么”（走向量）和“退货率多少”（走 SQL）两个子问题，各取所长后合并作答；③ 判据：路由不靠猜——给每个引擎清晰描述，再用一批带标注的问题评测路由命中率，错分多就改描述或加示例。一句话：别让一个引擎硬扛两类活，按数据形态分流。🔑 Key: use RouterQueryEngine to split by “question type” — text lookups to vectors, number-crunching to SQL — and when one question needs both, decompose it into sub-questions answered separately, then merge (echoing L18's routing and L30's query decomposition). (1) Route: give the Router two tools — a “document vector engine” and a “text-to-SQL engine” — each with a crisp capability description (“good at policy/clause semantic Q&A” vs “good at exact stats over orders/metrics”), and let the LLM selector pick per question; (2) decompose: use SubQuestionQueryEngine to split the compound question into “what is the policy” (→ vectors) and “what's the return rate” (→ SQL), then combine; (3) judge it: don't route by guesswork — give each engine a clear description and measure routing hit-rate on a labeled question set, fixing descriptions or adding examples when misrouted. In a line: don't make one engine carry both jobs — split by data shape.
🎯 3. 你要把 text-to-SQL 查询接口开放给外部用户。安全上你最担心什么？会怎么防？You're exposing a text-to-SQL interface to external users. What worries you most on security, and how do you defend it?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：text-to-SQL 在真的执行 LLM 生成的 SQL，等于把“对你数据库下命令”的能力间接交给了提问者——提示注入可诱导出 DROP/DELETE/越权读表。核心防线是“最小权限 + 隔离 + 限面 + 校验”，绝不靠“在提示词里求它别乱来”。① 只读、最小权限账号：只 SELECT、不能写、只授权该看的表/视图，从根上堵掉破坏与越权；② 限定可见面：include_tables / 业务视图把暴露的表/列收到最小，敏感列根本不进 schema；③ 沙箱 / 超时 / 行数上限：查询跑在隔离环境，加语句超时、LIMIT 和结果行数上限，防爆库；④ 执行前校验：对生成的 SQL 做白名单校验（只允许 SELECT、只允许这些表），可疑就拒；⑤ Pandas 更甚：PandasQueryEngine 会 eval Python、风险更大，core 0.14.22 已把它移到 llama-index-experimental 并标注“仅安全环境”，对外场景能不用就不用。🔑 Key: text-to-SQL actually executes LLM-generated SQL, so you've indirectly handed “issue commands to your database” to the asker — prompt injection can elicit DROP/DELETE/unauthorized reads. The real defense is “least privilege + isolation + a small surface + validation”, never “asking it nicely in the prompt”. (1) read-only, least-privilege account: SELECT only, no writes, granted just the tables/views it should see — closing destruction and over-reach at the root; (2) shrink the visible surface: include_tables / business views expose the minimum tables/columns; sensitive columns never enter the schema; (3) sandbox / timeouts / row caps: run queries in isolation with statement timeouts, LIMIT and result-row caps to prevent blowups; (4) validate before executing: allow-list the generated SQL (SELECT only, these tables only) and reject anything suspicious; (5) Pandas is worse: PandasQueryEngine evals Python and is riskier — core 0.14.22 has moved it to llama-index-experimental marked “secure environments only”, so avoid it for external-facing use.
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 为什么 PandasQueryEngine 要特别小心？（提示：它会执行 LLM 生成的 Python / 提示注入 · 越权 / 沙箱 · 只读 · 最小权限）Why must you be especially careful with PandasQueryEngine? (Hint: it executes LLM-generated Python / prompt injection · over-reach / sandbox · read-only · least privilege)
第七部分 · 超越文本 RAG

29 · 多模态 RAG

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

前面所有检索都是“文字找文字”：把问题和文本块塞进同一个向量空间，取回最相似的片段。可现实里大量知识长在图里——架构图、仪表盘截图、产品照、扫描的电路图。只把它们 OCR / 配文字成纯文本，视觉细节就丢了（“这张图里设备有几个接口”光靠文字答不出）。多模态 RAG 换一种存法：用多模态 embedding 把图和文映进同一个向量空间，于是能“用文字查图、用图查图”；检索时图和文一起召回，再交给一个看得见图的多模态 LLM 看着图作答。一句话：先让图文“坐标统一”，再让会看图的模型来回答。Every retrieval so far has been “text finds text”: push the question and text chunks into one vector space and fetch the most similar. But in the real world a lot of knowledge lives in images — architecture diagrams, dashboard screenshots, product photos, scanned schematics. OCR-ing or captioning them into plain text throws away the visual detail (“how many ports does the device in this picture have” can't be answered from text alone). Multimodal RAG stores things differently: a multimodal embedding maps images and text into the same vector space, so you can “query images with text, or query images with images”; retrieval recalls images and text together, then hands them to a vision-capable multimodal LLM that answers by actually looking at the picture. In a line: unify the coordinates of image and text first, then let a model that can see answer.

图文进同一向量空间：于是能“用文字查图、用图查图”Image and text in one vector space: now you can “query images with text, or with images”

纯文本 RAG 能成立，靠的是一个前提：问题和文档块被同一个 embedding 模型映进同一个向量空间，所以“算两段文字的余弦相似度、取最近邻”才有意义。多模态的关键，是把这个前提扩展到图像：用图文对训练出来的多模态 embedding（最有名的是 CLIP），会让“一张猫的照片”和“cat 这个词”落在彼此邻近的坐标上——图和文共用一套坐标系。一旦共用，跨模态的最近邻就有了意义：拿“文字问题”的向量，去和图像向量比距离，就能召回“画的就是这件事”的图片——这正是“用文字查图”的全部底气。反过来，如果图、文各在两个互不相干的空间，跨空间比距离毫无意义，就像拿经纬度去和体温比大小。所以“同一向量空间”不是一句口号，而是跨模态检索能不能成立的根。
Text-only RAG works because of one premise: the question and the doc chunks are mapped by the same embedding model into the same vector space, so “cosine similarity between two pieces of text, take the nearest” actually means something. The crux of going multimodal is extending that premise to images: a multimodal embedding trained on image–text pairs (the famous one is CLIP) makes “a photo of a cat” and “the word cat” land at neighboring coordinates — image and text share one coordinate system. Once shared, cross-modal nearest-neighbor becomes meaningful: take the vector of a text question, measure its distance to image vectors, and you recall the picture that “depicts exactly this” — which is the entire basis of “querying images with text”. Conversely, if image and text sat in two unrelated spaces, measuring distance across them would be meaningless, like comparing latitude to body temperature. So “the same vector space” isn't a slogan; it's the root of whether cross-modal retrieval can exist at all.
文本路径Text path
文字 → 文本 embedding
text → text embedding
vs
图像路径Image path
图片 → 图像 embedding
image → image embedding
两条路径映到同一向量空间，于是能跨模态互相检索both map into the same vector space, enabling cross-modal retrieval

建多模态索引：文本库、图像库各一，统一检索Build a multimodal index: a text store and an image store, retrieved together

把图文放进同一空间后，索引也要相应地分两套向量库。MultiModalVectorStoreIndex 内部维护两个 store：一个存文本节点（段落，走文本 embedding），一个存图像节点（ImageNode，走图像 embedding）。SimpleDirectoryReader 读一个混合文件夹时，文本读成普通 Document、图片读成 ImageDocument，from_documents 自动按类型分流进各自的 store。查询时两个 store 都召回，再把图、文候选合并交给下游——所以一次检索既可能捞回相关段落，也可能捞回相关图片。为什么要分两套、而不是混成一堆？因为两种模态的向量来自不同的 embedder，分库便于各自索引、各自调 top-k，最后在统一的检索结果里汇合。
Once image and text share a space, the index splits into two vector stores to match. MultiModalVectorStoreIndex keeps two stores internally: one for text nodes (passages, via the text embedding) and one for image nodes (ImageNode, via the image embedding). When SimpleDirectoryReader reads a mixed folder, text becomes ordinary Documents and pictures become ImageDocuments, and from_documents automatically routes each type into its own store. At query time both stores are queried and the image + text candidates are merged for the downstream step — so one retrieval may pull back relevant passages and relevant pictures alike. Why two stores rather than one mixed pile? Because the two modalities' vectors come from different embedders; separate stores let each be indexed and top-k-tuned independently, then meet in one unified result set.
子库Sub-store存什么Holds用什么 embeddingEmbedded by
文本 storeText store文本节点（段落）text nodes (passages)文本 embedding（沿用前课的标准文本嵌入，同属集成）text embedding (the standard text embedder from L08 — also an integration)
图像 storeImage store图像节点 ImageNodeimage nodes ImageNode图像 embedding（如 CLIP，走集成）image embedding (e.g. CLIP, an integration)
读混合文件夹建多模态索引：文本/图像各进一个 store，查询交多模态 LLM 看图作答Build a multimodal index from a mixed folder: text/images go to separate stores; the query hands it to a multimodal LLM to read the picture
from llama_index.core import SimpleDirectoryReader
from llama_index.core.indices import MultiModalVectorStoreIndex

documents = SimpleDirectoryReader("./mixed_docs").load_data()   # 文本 + 图片
index = MultiModalVectorStoreIndex.from_documents(documents)
qe = index.as_query_engine(llm=mm_llm)                          # mm_llm：多模态 LLM（走集成）
print(qe.query("图里这台设备的型号和接口数量是多少？"))
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
indices/multi_modal/base.py · MultiModalVectorStoreIndex — 文本与图像各建向量库，统一检索。separate text/image vector stores, retrieved together.
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
llama-index-embeddings-clip · ClipEmbedding — CLIP 图像 embedding 在 core 之外的集成包里——core 只给抽象；作答的视觉 LLM 同样是外部集成。the CLIP image embedding lives in an integration package outside core — core only ships the abstractions; the vision LLM is likewise an external integration.

检索件 + 生成件，都要换成多模态版Both the retrieval side and the generation side must go multimodal

把一套纯文本 RAG 升级成多模态，要同时换两个件，缺一不可。① 检索件：embedding 必须是多模态的，图片才能被编码进那个共享空间、被文字查到——这一步落在图像 embedding（如 CLIP）和索引里的图像 store 上。② 生成件：作答的 LLM 必须看得见图——检索召回的是图片节点，得交给一个多模态 LLM（视觉模型），它把图像当输入直接“看”着回答；换成纯文本 LLM，召回的图它根本读不了，多模态就白做了。还要分清哪是 core、哪是集成：抽象层是 core 的——MultiModalLLM 基类、MultiModalVectorStoreIndex、ImageNode 都在核心里；但具体能跑的模型——一个会看图的多模态 LLM（如 GPT-4o / Gemini）、CLIP 图像 embedding——都在 core 之外的集成包，要按需另装。core 给“插槽”，模型是“插件”。
Upgrading a text-only RAG to multimodal means swapping two components at once, neither optional. (1) Retrieval side: the embedding must be multimodal so images get encoded into that shared space and become findable by text — this rides on the image embedding (e.g. CLIP) and the index's image store. (2) Generation side: the answering LLM must be able to see the image — retrieval returns image nodes, which must go to a multimodal LLM (a vision model) that takes the image as input and actually “looks” to answer; swap in a text-only LLM and it simply can't read the recalled pictures, wasting the whole effort. Keep what is core vs an integration straight: the abstraction layer is core — the MultiModalLLM base class, MultiModalVectorStoreIndex and ImageNode all live in core; but the concrete runnable models — a vision-capable multimodal LLM (e.g. GPT-4o / Gemini), the CLIP image embedding — sit in integration packages outside core and are installed as needed. Core gives the “sockets”, the models are the “plugins”.
问题（文/图）query (text/img)
→
跨模态检索cross-modal retrieve
图+文都召回images + text
→
多模态 LLMmultimodal LLM
看图作答reads images
→
答案answer
多模态 RAG：检索召回图与文，再交会看图的 LLM 合成multimodal RAG: retrieve images+text, then a vision-capable LLM synthesizes

什么时候值得上多模态、什么时候不必When multimodal is worth it, and when it isn't

判断只看一件事：答案到底在不在“像素里”。值得上的典型场景，是信息只长在图里且文字旁注补不全的：读图表 / 仪表盘截图取趋势与数值、看产品照认型号与接口、查电路图 / 架构图 / 扫描件里的连接与标注——这些问题“看图才能答”，纯文本 RAG 结构上答不了。反过来，如果图只是装饰、或它的信息本就写在正文 / 标题 / 配文里，那纯文本检索又快又便宜，没必要上多模态。成本也要算清：多模态 embedding 和视觉 LLM 更贵更慢、图像 store 也更占资源。还有一种降级方案——先把图 OCR / 配成 caption 文字、再做纯文本 RAG：便宜，但丢视觉细节（布局、颜色、相对位置、图里没写成字的东西）。实务里的稳妥姿态是默认文本优先、图像按需启用：只对“确有图、且要看图”的查询和文档走多模态。
The test is one thing: does the answer actually live “in the pixels”. The cases worth it are where information exists only in the image and no text caption fully covers it: reading charts / dashboard screenshots for trends and values, reading a product photo for a model number and ports, checking a schematic / architecture diagram / scan for connections and labels — these need you to “look at the picture”, and text-only RAG structurally can't answer them. Conversely, if the image is merely decorative, or its information is already written in the body / heading / caption, then text-only retrieval is faster and cheaper and multimodal isn't needed. Count the cost too: multimodal embeddings and vision LLMs are pricier and slower, and an image store consumes more resources. There's also a downgrade path — OCR/caption the image into text first, then do text-only RAG: cheap, but it loses visual detail (layout, color, relative position, anything not written out in the picture). The safe production stance is text-first by default, images enabled on demand: route only the queries and documents that “truly have an image and need to look at it” through the multimodal path.
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
想象给每张照片和每个词都标上同一张地图上的坐标：一旦“猫的照片”和“猫”这个词被放到地图上同一个点，你就能站在词上、找最近的照片——这就是“用文字查图”。要是照片用的是一张地图、文字用的是另一张互不对齐的地图，那“谁离谁近”就无从谈起。多模态 embedding 干的就是“把图和字标到同一张地图上”这件事；剩下的检索，不过是在同一张图上找最近的点。
Picture giving every photo and every word coordinates on the same map: once “a photo of a cat” and the word “cat” are placed at the same spot, you can stand on the word and find the nearest photo — that's “querying images with text”. If photos used one map and words used another, misaligned map, then “who is near whom” is meaningless. A multimodal embedding does exactly the “plot images and words on one shared map” part; the retrieval that follows is just finding the nearest point on that one map.
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 多模态 RAG 的根：用多模态 embedding（如 CLIP）把图和文映进同一向量空间，跨模态最近邻才有意义，于是能“用文字查图、用图查图”。The root of multimodal RAG: a multimodal embedding (e.g. CLIP) maps images and text into the same vector space, making cross-modal nearest-neighbor meaningful — so you can “query images with text, or with images”.
  • MultiModalVectorStoreIndex 内部文本 store + 图像 store 各一，from_documents 按类型分流（文本 → Document、图片 → ImageDocument），查询时两库都召回再合并。MultiModalVectorStoreIndex keeps a text store and an image store; from_documents routes by type (text → Document, image → ImageDocument), and a query recalls from both stores and merges.
  • 升级要同时换两个件：检索件换多模态 embedding，生成件换看得见图的多模态 LLM；纯文本 LLM 读不了召回的图。Upgrading swaps two components at once: a multimodal embedding on the retrieval side and a vision-capable multimodal LLM on the generation side; a text-only LLM can't read the recalled images.
  • core 给抽象、集成给模型：MultiModalVectorStoreIndex / MultiModalLLM / ImageNode 在 core；会看图的多模态 LLM（如 GPT-4o / Gemini）、CLIP embedding 在集成包。按需上多模态——答案在像素里才值得，否则文本优先更省。Core ships abstractions, integrations ship models: MultiModalVectorStoreIndex / MultiModalLLM / ImageNode are in core; a vision-capable multimodal LLM (e.g. GPT-4o / Gemini) and the CLIP embedding are in integration packages. Go multimodal on demand — worth it only when the answer is in the pixels, otherwise text-first is cheaper.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
多模态 RAG 的精髓，是把“找相似”从纯文本扩展到图文之间，而这一切的支点只有一个：图和文落在同一个向量空间。有了这层跨模态对齐，“用文字查图”才从不可能变成一次普通的最近邻；没有它，图像向量和文本向量就是两套不能互比的坐标。工程上要记住三件事：① 两个件一起换——检索端的多模态 embedding 让图进得了空间，生成端的视觉 LLM 让模型看得懂召回的图，缺一边都不成；② 分清 core 与集成——core 只给 MultiModalVectorStoreIndex / MultiModalLLM 这层抽象插槽，真正能跑的视觉模型和 CLIP embedding 是外部集成，别把它们当核心内置；③ 按需启用——多模态更贵更慢，只有当“答案确实在像素里”时才值得，否则文本优先、必要时再用 caption 降级。一句话：先让图文坐标统一，再让会看图的模型来回答。
The essence of multimodal RAG is extending “find similar” from pure text to between images and text, and the whole thing pivots on one fulcrum: images and text landing in the same vector space. With that cross-modal alignment, “querying images with text” turns from impossible into an ordinary nearest-neighbor; without it, image vectors and text vectors are two coordinate systems you can't compare. Three engineering points: (1) swap both components together — the retrieval-side multimodal embedding lets images enter the space, the generation-side vision LLM lets the model understand the recalled images, and neither alone suffices; (2) keep core vs integrations straight — core ships only the abstraction sockets like MultiModalVectorStoreIndex / MultiModalLLM, while the actual runnable vision models and CLIP embedding are external integrations, not core built-ins; (3) enable on demand — multimodal is pricier and slower, worth it only when “the answer is truly in the pixels”, otherwise go text-first and fall back to captioning when needed. In a line: unify the coordinates of image and text first, then let a model that can see answer.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. 多模态 RAG 能“用文字查图”的根本前提是什么？What is the fundamental prerequisite that lets multimodal RAG “query images with text”?
  1. 换一个更大参数量的 LLMswitch to an LLM with more parameters
  2. 先把每张图用 caption 转成文字再做纯文本检索caption every image into text first, then do text-only retrieval
  3. 图和文被映射到同一个向量空间images and text are mapped into the same vector space
  4. 关闭 rerank 重排turn off reranking
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：CAnswer: C 正确的是“图和文被映射到同一个向量空间”：跨模态检索的前提，是图、文的 embedding 落在同一空间，才能拿文字向量去和图像向量比距离、互相召回。“先把图用 caption 转成文字再做纯文本检索”是另一种降级方案（能跑，但丢视觉细节），并没有让图文向量对齐；“换更大参数量的 LLM”和“关闭 rerank 重排”都在调别的环节，都不解决跨模态对齐这个根本前提。The right one is “images and text are mapped into the same vector space”: cross-modal retrieval hinges on image and text embeddings sitting in one shared space, so a text vector can be distance-compared to image vectors and recall them. “Caption images into text first, then do text-only retrieval” is a downgrade (it runs, but loses visual detail) and never aligns the image/text vectors; “use a larger LLM” and “turn off reranking” tweak other stages and none address the cross-modal alignment that is the real prerequisite.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 多模态 RAG 的 embedding 和视觉 LLM 都更贵更慢，图像 store 也更占资源。你会怎么权衡，别让每条查询都付这份钱？A multimodal RAG's embeddings and vision LLM are both pricier and slower, and the image store costs more. How would you weigh it so not every query pays that bill?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：默认文本优先、图像按需启用——只对“确有图、且要看图才能答”的查询和文档走多模态，别让每条请求都付视觉模型的钱。① 按文档分流：入库时区分“图承载信息”的文档（图表、截图、产品图）和“纯文字”文档，只给前者建图像 store、跑多模态 embedding；② 按查询分流：用路由（回想 L18）判断这条问题要不要看图——要，才召回图片、调多模态 LLM，否则走更快更省的纯文本路径；③ 降级兜底：很多场景先把图 OCR / 配 caption 成文字、再做文本 RAG 就够了，只在 caption 丢了关键视觉细节时才升级到真多模态；④ 用数字定阈值：统计“真正需要看图”的查询占比，对比多模态 vs 文本在这批问题上的答对率增量，是否抵得过多出的延迟与成本。一句话：多模态是按需的精装件，不是默认全开。🔑 Key: default to text-first and enable images on demand — route only the queries and documents that “truly have an image and need to look at it” through the multimodal path; don't make every request pay for a vision model. (1) Route by document: at ingest, separate “image-bearing” docs (charts, screenshots, product photos) from “text-only” ones, and build an image store / run multimodal embeddings only for the former; (2) route by query: use routing (recall L18) to decide whether a question needs to look at an image — if so, recall pictures and call the multimodal LLM, otherwise take the faster, cheaper text-only path; (3) downgrade fallback: in many cases OCR/captioning images into text and doing text RAG is enough, upgrading to true multimodal only when captioning drops key visual detail; (4) set the threshold with numbers: measure the share of queries that genuinely need the image, and compare multimodal vs text answer-accuracy lift on that subset against the extra latency and cost. In a line: multimodal is an on-demand upgrade, not on by default.
🎯 2. 评估多模态 RAG 和评估纯文本 RAG 有什么不同？你怎么证明多模态确实带来了价值？How does evaluating a multimodal RAG differ from evaluating a text-only one? How do you prove multimodal actually adds value?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：金标问答里必须包含一批“靠图才能答”的题——答案只在图里、文字旁注补不全，否则多模态和纯文本会打平，测不出它的价值（呼应 L19 评估、L22 回归集）。① 题目要对路：除常规问答外，专门设计“读图表取数值”“认产品图型号”“看架构图连接”这类必须看图的题，纯文本基线在这批题上应当明显答不好；② 分轨看指标：检索侧看“相关图片有没有被召回”（图像命中率），生成侧看视觉 LLM 读图后的 Faithfulness / 正确率，别把两者混成一个分；③ 和文本基线对照：同一批题跑“纯文本 RAG” vs “多模态 RAG”，用答对率的增量证明多模态值这个钱；④ 接回归闸：把这批“看图题”固定成回归集，挡住“换了 embedding / 模型把读图能力悄悄弄坏”的退化。一句话：测不出差异，往往是题目里根本没有需要看图的题。🔑 Key: the gold Q&A set must include a batch of “only answerable from the image” questions — the answer lives only in the picture and no caption covers it — otherwise multimodal and text-only tie and you can't measure the value (echoing L19's evaluation, L22's regression set). (1) Questions on point: beyond ordinary Q&A, deliberately design “read a value off a chart”, “identify a product model from a photo”, “trace connections in an architecture diagram” items that require looking at the image, on which a text-only baseline should clearly do poorly; (2) metrics by track: on the retrieval side check “were the relevant images recalled” (image hit-rate), on the generation side check the vision LLM's Faithfulness / correctness after reading the image — don't blend them into one score; (3) compare against a text baseline: run “text-only RAG” vs “multimodal RAG” on the same set and use the accuracy lift to prove multimodal earns its cost; (4) wire a regression gate: freeze those “look-at-the-image” questions into a regression set to block “swapping the embedding / model quietly broke image reading” regressions. In a line: if you can't measure a difference, usually the set has no questions that actually need the image.
🎯 3. 有人说“把图都转成 caption 文字、再做纯文本 RAG”就够了，不必上真多模态。你怎么看这个取舍？Someone argues “just caption all images into text and do text-only RAG” is enough, no need for true multimodal. How do you see this trade-off?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：caption / OCR 降级法便宜又好维护，能覆盖“信息一句话能说清”的图；但把图压成文字就丢了视觉细节，所以选型取决于你的图是“配文字就够”还是“非看原图不可”。① caption 够用的场景：图里的信息本就能被一段描述覆盖（写着规格的表格、一句话能说清的示意图），转成文字后纯文本 RAG 又快又省，还能复用现成的文本检索栈；② 必须真多模态的场景：答案藏在布局 / 颜色 / 相对位置 / 没写成字的细节里（电路怎么连、仪表盘哪条线在涨、产品照上有几个接口），caption 几乎必然漏，得让图进共享向量空间、再交视觉 LLM 直接看；③ 成本对照：caption 省掉了图像 embedding 和视觉 LLM 的开销，但 caption 本身要花一次模型调用且质量参差；真多模态更贵更慢但信息无损。一句话：caption 是有损压缩，能不能用先问“丢掉的那部分要不要紧”。🔑 Key: the caption/OCR downgrade is cheap and easy to maintain and covers images whose “information fits in a sentence”; but squashing an image into text drops visual detail, so the choice depends on whether your images are “fine with a caption” or “must be seen in the original”. (1) When captioning suffices: the image's information is already coverable by a description (a spec table, a one-sentence schematic), so converting to text and doing text RAG is fast and cheap and reuses your existing text retrieval stack; (2) when true multimodal is required: the answer hides in layout / color / relative position / details never written as words (how a circuit connects, which line on a dashboard is rising, how many ports are on a product photo), where captioning almost certainly misses, so the image must enter the shared vector space and go to a vision LLM to be seen directly; (3) cost contrast: captioning saves the image-embedding and vision-LLM cost, but the caption itself takes a model call of uneven quality; true multimodal is pricier and slower but lossless. In a line: captioning is lossy compression — first ask “does the part it drops matter”.

💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • 纯文字 RAG 遇到“这张架构图说明了什么”为什么无能为力、多模态怎么解决？（提示：视觉细节 / 同一向量空间 / 会看图的 LLM）Why is text-only RAG helpless on “what does this architecture diagram show”, and how does multimodal solve it? (Hint: visual detail / same vector space / a vision-capable LLM)
第七部分 · 超越文本 RAG

30 · 查询分解 Sub-Question

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

到这里，检索路径上的每一课都默认同一个形状：一个问题 → 一次检索 → 取回 top-k → 合成答案。可现实里有一整类问题，单次 top-k 天生答不全——“2023 的营收比 2022 增长了多少”“对比 A、B 两份合同的违约条款差异”“先查 X 是什么、再查它的兼容机型”。这些是对比 / 跨源 / 多步问题：答案不在某一段话里现成写着，而要分别查好几处、再把结果合起来。单次检索要么只召回一边（漏掉另一边），要么把两边混在一起（固定的 top-k 名额被一方挤占）。SubQuestionQueryEngine 换一种思路：先让 LLM 把母问题拆成几个子问题，每个子问题路由到对应的查询引擎工具各自检索，最后把子答案汇总成一个答案。一句话：别让一次 top-k 硬扛对比题，拆成子问分别查、再合并。Every lesson on the retrieval path so far assumed one shape: one question → one retrieval → fetch top-k → synthesize. But a whole class of questions can't be answered by a single top-k — “how much did revenue grow in 2023 vs 2022”, “compare the breach clauses in contracts A and B”, “first find what X is, then find its compatible models”. These are comparison / cross-source / multi-step questions: the answer isn't sitting ready in any one passage but must be looked up in several places and combined. A single retrieval either recalls only one side (missing the other) or mixes both into one bucket (the fixed top-k slots crowded out by one side). SubQuestionQueryEngine flips the approach: first an LLM splits the parent question into sub-questions, each routed to its matching query-engine tool to retrieve on its own, and finally the sub-answers are aggregated into one answer. In a line: don't make a single top-k carry a comparison; split into sub-questions, retrieve each, then combine.

痛点：对比 / 跨源 / 多步问题，单次 top-k 答不全The pain: comparison / cross-source / multi-step questions a single top-k can't answer

朴素 RAG 的检索是“一次性”的：把问题编码成一个向量，取回最相似的 top-k 个片段，再让 LLM 据此作答。对“X 的退款政策是什么”这种单点问题，这一次检索就够了。但碰到“2023 比 2022 营收增长多少”，麻烦立刻显现：答案要同时拿到“2023 营收”和“2022 营收”两个事实、再相减，而它们往往分散在两份文档（两年的财报）里。单次 top-k 只有固定的几个名额：要么向量更偏向其中一年、把另一年挤出召回（漏一边），要么两年的片段混进同一批、彼此稀释，关键数字反而没进前 k（混在一起）。跨源问题（“我们的产品和竞品在 X 上谁更强”要查两套资料）、并行多部分问题（“把 2021、2022、2023 三年的营收各查一遍再汇总”——几个子问彼此独立、可并行）也都是同一个结构性短板：一个问题里其实藏着好几个独立的检索需求，硬塞进一次 top-k 必然顾此失彼。
Plain RAG's retrieval is “one-shot”: encode the question into a vector, fetch the top-k most similar chunks, then let the LLM answer from them. For a single-point question like “what is X's refund policy”, that one retrieval suffices. But ask “how much did revenue grow in 2023 vs 2022” and the trouble shows immediately: the answer needs two facts at once — “2023 revenue” and “2022 revenue” — then a subtraction, and those usually sit in two different documents (two years' reports). A single top-k has only a few fixed slots: either the vector leans toward one year and crowds the other out of recall (missing one side), or both years' chunks land in the same batch and dilute each other so the key number never makes the top-k (mixed together). Cross-source questions (“are we or the competitor stronger on X” needs two sets of material) and parallel multi-part questions (“look up revenue for 2021, 2022 and 2023 each, then combine” — the sub-questions are independent and run in parallel) share the same structural weakness: one question actually hides several independent retrieval needs, and forcing them into one top-k inevitably shortchanges some.

问“2023 比 2022 增长多少”，固定名额里两年的营收互相挤占——要么漏一年，要么都没进前 k
ask “growth 2023 vs 2022” and the two years' revenue crowd each other in the fixed slots — miss one year, or neither makes the top-k

Sub-QuestionSub-Question
拆成“2023 营收？”“2022 营收？”两个子问，各查各的文档，都召回后再相减
split into “2023 revenue?” and “2022 revenue?”, retrieve each from its own doc, recall both, then subtract
同一个对比题：单次 top-k 顾此失彼，Sub-Question 拆开各查再合并Same comparison: a single top-k shortchanges one side; Sub-Question splits, retrieves each, then combines

SubQuestion：拆母问题 → 路由到各工具 → 各自检索 → 汇总SubQuestion: split the parent → route to tools → retrieve each → aggregate

SubQuestionQueryEngine 把“一次检索”换成“先拆、再分别查、最后合”四步。① 拆：把母问题连同每个工具的名字与描述一起交给 LLM，让它生成一组子问题，并为每个子问题指定该用哪个工具（这一步是 LLM 驱动的）；② 路由：每个子问题被发往它对应的 QueryEngineTool——工具其实就是“一个查询引擎 + 一段说明它擅长什么的 metadata”，描述写得准不准，直接决定子问会不会被送对地方；③ 各自检索：每个工具在自己的数据上独立跑一次检索与作答，互不干扰，于是“2023 营收”只在 2023 的库里找、“2022 营收”只在 2022 的库里找；④ 汇总：引擎把所有子问题的答案收集起来，作为上下文交给 LLM 合成最终答案（比如把两年的营收相减）。关键在于：母问题里“藏着的几个检索需求”被显式拆成了独立的几次检索，每一次都拥有自己完整的top-k 名额，谁也不挤占谁。注意：Sub-Question 是一次性并行拆解，不能把某个子答案回填进下一个子问；真正“前一步答案喂下一步”的依赖链要交给 Agent（见 L32）。
SubQuestionQueryEngine replaces “one retrieval” with four steps — split, route, retrieve separately, combine. (1) Split: hand the parent question plus each tool's name and description to the LLM and have it generate a set of sub-questions, each tagged with which tool to use (this step is LLM-driven); (2) route: each sub-question goes to its matching QueryEngineTool — a tool is just “a query engine plus metadata describing what it's good at”, and how accurately that description is written directly decides whether the sub-question is sent to the right place; (3) retrieve separately: each tool runs its own retrieval and answer over its own data independently, so “2023 revenue” is sought only in the 2023 store and “2022 revenue” only in the 2022 store; (4) aggregate: the engine collects every sub-answer and feeds them as context to the LLM to synthesize the final answer (e.g. subtract the two years). The key: the “several retrieval needs hidden in the parent” are made explicit as several independent retrievals, each with its own full top-k budget, none crowding out another. Note: Sub-Question splits once, in parallel — it cannot feed one sub-answer into the next sub-question; a true dependent chain (step 2 needs step 1's answer) belongs to an Agent (see L32).
两个引擎各包成带 description 的工具，SubQuestion 自动拆问、路由、各查、汇总——描述决定路由Wrap each engine as a tool with a description; SubQuestion auto-splits, routes, retrieves each, aggregates — the description drives routing
from llama_index.core.query_engine import SubQuestionQueryEngine
from llama_index.core.tools import QueryEngineTool, ToolMetadata

tools = [
    QueryEngineTool(query_engine=qe_2022, metadata=ToolMetadata(name="y2022", description="2022 年财报")),
    QueryEngineTool(query_engine=qe_2023, metadata=ToolMetadata(name="y2023", description="2023 年财报")),
]
engine = SubQuestionQueryEngine.from_defaults(query_engine_tools=tools)
print(engine.query("2023 年的营收比 2022 年增长了多少？"))   # 自动拆成两个子问题再相减

一个母问题并行扇出到多个数据源工具，再收敛成一个答案（子问彼此独立、并行）one parent question fans out in parallel to several source tools, then converges to one answer (the sub-questions are independent and parallel)

与 L18 的区别：换更强的检索器 vs 拆问题 + 多引擎编排vs L18: a stronger retriever vs decomposing the question + orchestrating engines

这一课很容易和 L18 的进阶检索搞混，但两者其实在不同维度上发力。L18（混合检索、rerank、HyDE）解决的是“同一次检索，怎么找得更准”——它换的是检索器本身：多一路 BM25、加一层交叉编码器精排、先造个假设文档再查，目标是让那一批 top-k 的质量更高。但无论检索器多强，它仍是“一个问题、一次检索”——对“2023 比 2022 增长多少”这种内含多个子需求的问题，再准的单次召回也答不全。SubQuestion 动的是另一个维度：它不改检索器，而是改“检索的次数与编排”——把一个问题拆成多个子问题、分别路由到多个引擎、最后汇总。所以两者正交、可叠加：每个子问题底下，完全可以挂一个用了 L18 全套（混合 + rerank）的强检索引擎——SubQuestion 负责“拆对、问对引擎”，L18 负责“每一问都查得准”。
This lesson is easy to confuse with L18's advanced retrieval, but the two work on different axes. L18 (hybrid retrieval, rerank, HyDE) solves “within one retrieval, how to find more accurately” — it swaps the retriever itself: add a BM25 path, layer on a cross-encoder rerank, draft a hypothetical document first — all to make that one batch of top-k higher quality. But however strong the retriever, it's still “one question, one retrieval” — and for a question like “growth 2023 vs 2022” that hides several sub-needs, even a perfect single recall can't answer it fully. SubQuestion moves a different axis: it doesn't change the retriever, it changes “how many retrievals and how they're orchestrated” — splitting one question into sub-questions, routing each to a different engine, and aggregating. So the two are orthogonal and stackable: under each sub-question you can absolutely hang a strong engine running L18's full kit (hybrid + rerank) — SubQuestion handles “split right, ask the right engine”, L18 handles “each question retrieves accurately”.
对比项AspectL18 进阶检索L18 advanced retrievalL30 Sub-QuestionL30 Sub-Question
解决的问题Solves一次检索怎么找得更准how one retrieval finds more accurately多需求问题怎么答得全how a multi-need question gets answered fully
改动对象What it changes检索器（+BM25 / +rerank / +HyDE）the retriever (+BM25 / +rerank / +HyDE)检索的次数与编排（拆 + 路由 + 汇总）count & orchestration of retrievals (split + route + aggregate)
检索次数Retrievals一次one多次（每个子问一次）many (one per sub-question)
最擅长Best at单点问题召回得更精准single-point questions, more precise recall对比 / 跨源 / 多步问题comparison / cross-source / multi-step questions
🧩 生活类比🧩 Analogy
像做一道复杂的大题：与其抱着一本书从头翻到尾、想一次找全（单次 top-k），不如先把大题拆成几个小问——“2023 年营收是多少？”“2022 年营收是多少？”——分别翻到对应的那一章查清楚，最后把两个小答案合起来相减得出大题的答案。复杂问题难的从来不是某一小步，而是“得分头查好几处再合并”；SubQuestion 干的就是替你拆题、分头查、再合卷。
Like solving a hard exam problem: rather than thumbing through one whole book hoping to find everything in a single pass (one top-k), first break it into small questions — “what was 2023 revenue?”, “what was 2022 revenue?” — look each up in its own chapter, then combine and subtract the two small answers into the big one. The hard part of a complex question was never any single step but “looking several places up separately and merging”; SubQuestion does exactly that for you — split, look up separately, then collate.
✅ 本课要点✅ Key points
  • 对比 / 跨源 / 多步问题，单次 top-k 天生答不全——要么漏一边，要么两边混在一起挤占名额。Comparison / cross-source / multi-step questions are inherently beyond a single top-k — it misses one side or mixes both and crowds the slots.
  • SubQuestionQueryEngine：LLM 把母问题拆成子问题 → 每个子问路由到对应 QueryEngineTool → 各自检索作答 → 汇总成最终答案。SubQuestionQueryEngine: the LLM splits the parent into sub-questions → each routes to its matching QueryEngineTool → each retrieves and answers → aggregate into the final answer.
  • QueryEngineTool = 查询引擎 + ToolMetadata（name / description）；description 写准与否直接决定子问路由对不对。A QueryEngineTool = a query engine + ToolMetadata (name / description); how accurately the description is written directly decides whether a sub-question routes correctly.
  • 与 L18 正交：L18 换更强的检索器（让一次检索更准），SubQuestion 改检索的次数与编排（拆 + 路由 + 汇总）；子问底下可叠加 L18 强引擎。Orthogonal to L18: L18 swaps in a stronger retriever (one retrieval, more accurate), SubQuestion changes the count and orchestration of retrievals (split + route + aggregate); you can stack an L18 engine under each sub-question.
💡 设计亮点💡 Design insight
Sub-Question 的精髓，是把检索从“一个问题配一次 top-k”升级成“一个问题配一套检索计划”。朴素 RAG 默认每个问题只对应一次召回，于是凡是内含多个独立事实的问题——对比、跨源、多步——都被那固定的 top-k 名额卡住：召回一方就漏另一方。Sub-Question 让 LLM 先把问题拆解成几个能被单独回答的子问，每个子问拥有自己完整的检索预算、被路由到最懂它的引擎，最后再汇总——本质上是把“检索”从一个固定动作，变成了一段可由 LLM 规划的编排。要记住三件事：① 它和 L18 正交——L18 让每一次检索更准，Sub-Question 决定要检索几次、各问谁，两者叠加最强；② 成本是实打实多花的——拆问要一次 LLM 调用，n 个子问就是 n 次检索 + 多次生成，延迟和 token 都翻几倍，别为单点问题滥用；③ 路由的命脉是工具的description——描述写歪了，子问就被送错引擎，再好的拆解也白费。一句话：当一个问题其实是好几个问题时，先替它拆题、分头查、再合并。它也为后面的 Router（选一条路）与 Agent（动态多步循环）埋下伏笔——同样是“编排多个能力”，只是编排的灵活度一路递增。
The essence of Sub-Question is upgrading retrieval from “one question, one top-k” to “one question, a retrieval plan”. Plain RAG assumes each question maps to a single recall, so any question hiding several independent facts — comparison, cross-source, multi-step — gets stuck in those fixed top-k slots: recall one side and you miss the other. Sub-Question has the LLM first decompose the question into sub-questions that can each be answered on their own, give each its own full retrieval budget routed to the engine that knows it best, then aggregate — turning “retrieval” from one fixed action into an orchestration the LLM can plan. Remember three things: (1) it's orthogonal to L18 — L18 makes each retrieval more accurate, Sub-Question decides how many retrievals and whom to ask; stacked, they're strongest; (2) the cost is real and additive — splitting takes an LLM call, and n sub-questions mean n retrievals plus several generations, multiplying latency and tokens, so don't overuse it on single-point questions; (3) routing lives or dies by the tool's description — write it wrong and sub-questions go to the wrong engine, wasting even a perfect split. In a line: when one question is really several, split it, look each up separately, then combine. It also sets up the later Router (pick one path) and Agent (a dynamic multi-step loop) — all “orchestrating multiple capabilities”, just with steadily rising flexibility.

🧪 自测 · 想一想为什么这么设计🧪 Self-check · think about the design

1. SubQuestionQueryEngine 最擅长哪类问题？Which kind of question is SubQuestionQueryEngine best at?
  1. 压缩 prompt 省 tokencompressing the prompt to save tokens
  2. 单文档里的相似检索similarity retrieval inside a single document
  3. 流式逐字输出streaming the output token by token
  4. 跨多个来源的对比或多步问题comparison or multi-step questions across multiple sources
看答案与解析Show answer & explanation 点击展开expand
答案：DAnswer: D 正确的是“跨多个来源的对比或多步问题”：sub-question 的价值正是把这类问题拆成子问、分别检索、再汇总，补上单次 top-k 答不全的部分。“单文档里的相似检索”普通 retriever 一次召回就够，用不上拆解；“压缩 prompt 省 token”是省成本的关注点（拆问反而会多花 token），“流式逐字输出”是响应方式——两者都和“把复杂问题拆开”无关。The right one is “comparison or multi-step questions across multiple sources”: that's exactly sub-question's value — split such a question into sub-questions, retrieve each, then aggregate, covering what a single top-k can't. “Similarity retrieval inside a single document” is handled by an ordinary retriever in one recall and needs no decomposition; “compressing the prompt to save tokens” is a cost concern (splitting actually spends more tokens), and “streaming output token by token” is a delivery style — neither has anything to do with breaking a complex question apart.

🎯 面试官提问 · 试着答出要点🎯 Interviewer asks · cover the key points

🎯 1. 你的 SubQuestionQueryEngine 经常拆错——要么子问跑偏、答非所问，要么把一个简单问题拆成一堆没必要的子问。你会怎么定位并控住？Your SubQuestionQueryEngine often splits badly — sub-questions drift off-target, or a simple question gets shattered into needless sub-questions. How would you localize and rein it in?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：拆解和路由都由 LLM + 工具描述驱动，所以先把“工具 description 写准”（决定路由对不对），再限定子问数量、给每个子问加 trace 让它可观测（呼应 L23）。① 工具 description 写准：子问被送到哪个引擎，全看工具的 ToolMetadata.description——把每个工具“擅长什么、覆盖什么数据”写清楚、彼此边界不重叠，子问才不会被路由错（这是最常见的“跑偏”根因）；② 限定子问数量 / 收敛拆解：约束最多拆几个子问，避免把单点问题过度拆解，既省成本又减少噪声；③ 每个子问加 trace、可观测：接入 L23 的可观测（回调 / Phoenix 等），把“拆出了哪些子问、各路由到哪个工具、各自召回了什么”一条条打出来——拆错时一眼看出是“拆的步骤错”还是“某个子问检索错”，分而治之；④ 评估闭环：用一组多步 / 对比金标问题看端到端答案对不对，针对错例回去改工具描述或拆解提示。一句话：拆错先别怪模型，多半是工具描述没写清、或没给它可观测的眼睛。🔑 Key: both the split and the routing are driven by the LLM plus the tool descriptions, so first “get the tool descriptions right” (they decide whether routing is correct), then cap the number of sub-questions and add a trace to each so it's observable (echoing L23). (1) Write tool descriptions accurately: which engine a sub-question goes to depends entirely on each tool's ToolMetadata.description — state clearly what each tool is good at and which data it covers, with non-overlapping boundaries, so sub-questions don't get misrouted (the most common “drift” root cause); (2) cap the sub-question count / tame the split: constrain how many sub-questions can be produced, avoiding over-splitting a single-point question — saving cost and cutting noise; (3) add a trace to each sub-question: wire in L23's observability (callbacks / Phoenix, etc.) and print out “which sub-questions were produced, which tool each was routed to, what each recalled” — when it splits wrong you see at a glance whether it's “the split step” or “one sub-question's retrieval”, and divide and conquer; (4) an eval loop: use a set of multi-step / comparison gold questions, check end-to-end answer correctness, and fix tool descriptions or the split prompt on the failures. In a line: don't blame the model first — bad splits are usually unclear tool descriptions or missing observability.
🎯 2. SubQuestionQueryEngine 和 Router（L18）、Agent（L26/L32）听起来都在“编排多个引擎”。它们到底有什么区别？你会怎么按问题选？SubQuestionQueryEngine, a Router (L18) and an Agent (L26/L32) all sound like “orchestrating multiple engines”. What's the actual difference, and how would you choose by question?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：三者在“编排灵活度”上递增——Router 从多条路里选一条走；SubQuestion 一次把问题拆成多条、并行各查、再汇总（固定的一轮）；Agent 则动态循环多步，边做边决定下一步（为 L32 铺垫）。① Router（选一条）：一个问题 → 选择器挑最合适的那一个引擎/工具 → 走完即止；适合“这问题该归谁管”清晰、但本质还是单路的场景。② SubQuestion（拆多条、一轮汇总）：一个问题 → 拆成若干并行子问 → 各自检索 → 一次性汇总；适合“对比 / 跨源 / 多步但步骤可预先拆清”的问题，编排是固定的一轮、不回头。③ Agent（动态多步循环）：在一个 think → act → observe 的循环里，根据上一步结果再决定下一步，可调工具、可回退、可迭代；适合步骤事先不知道、要边走边定的开放任务，代价是更慢更贵更难控。怎么选：单路分流用 Router；能预先拆成几问、一轮合并用 SubQuestion；步骤不确定、需要反复试探才用 Agent——别用大锤敲钉子。🔑 Key: the three rise in “orchestration flexibility” — a Router picks one path among many; SubQuestion splits one question into several, retrieves them in parallel, then aggregates (a fixed single round); an Agent runs a dynamic multi-step loop, deciding the next step as it goes (setting up L32). (1) Router (pick one): one question → the selector picks the single most suitable engine/tool → done; good when “who should handle this” is clear but it's still single-path. (2) SubQuestion (split many, one-round aggregate): one question → split into several parallel sub-questions → retrieve each → aggregate once; good for comparison / cross-source / multi-step questions whose steps can be split up front, with a fixed single round and no looping back. (3) Agent (dynamic multi-step loop): inside a think → act → observe loop it decides the next step from the last result, calling tools, backtracking, iterating; good for open tasks whose steps aren't known in advance, at the cost of more latency, money and harder control. How to choose: single-path dispatch → Router; can be pre-split into a few questions merged in one round → SubQuestion; uncertain steps needing trial and error → Agent — don't swing a sledgehammer at a tack.

🎯 3. 上线后发现接入 SubQuestion 让延迟和成本明显上升。你会怎么判断“哪些查询真的需要拆”、把这份开销花在刀刃上？After launch you find SubQuestion noticeably raised latency and cost. How would you decide “which queries truly need splitting” and spend that overhead only where it pays off?
看参考要点Show key points 点击展开expand
🔑 重点：拆解不是免费的——一次拆题 LLM 调用 + n 个子问 = n 次检索 + 多次生成，单点问题根本不该走它；用“问题类型路由 + 数据定阈值”只把对比/多步问题送去拆。① 先分流再拆：用一个轻量分类/路由（回想 L18）判断问题是不是“对比 / 跨源 / 多步”——是才交给 SubQuestion，普通单点问题走一次普通检索就好，别让所有查询都付拆解的钱；② 限子问数量：约束最多拆几个子问，n 越大成本越线性上涨；③ 能并行就并行：子问之间无依赖时并行检索，能砍掉大部分串行延迟（真正的依赖链需要串行、按上一步结果决定下一步，那是 Agent 的活，不是 Sub-Question）；④ 用数据定阈值：统计真实流量里对比/多步问题的占比，对比“全走 SubQuestion vs 仅这一小撮走”的答对率增量与延迟/成本差，确认这份开销值得；⑤ 缓存子答案：高频子问（如“2022 营收”）可缓存复用。一句话：SubQuestion 是给“真有多个子需求”的问题用的精装件，别默认全开。🔑 Key: splitting isn't free — one split LLM call + n sub-questions = n retrievals plus several generations, so single-point questions shouldn't go through it at all; use “question-type routing + data-set thresholds” to send only comparison/multi-step questions to be split. (1) Route before splitting: a lightweight classifier/router (recall L18) decides whether a question is “comparison / cross-source / multi-step” — only then hand it to SubQuestion, while ordinary single-point questions take one plain retrieval; don't make every query pay the split tax; (2) cap the sub-question count: constrain how many sub-questions are allowed — cost rises roughly linearly with n; (3) parallelize when you can: when sub-questions are independent, retrieve them in parallel to cut most of the serial latency (a true dependent chain must run serially, deciding each step from the last result — that's an Agent's job, not Sub-Question's); (4) set the threshold with data: measure the share of comparison/multi-step questions in real traffic and compare “all through SubQuestion vs only that minority” on answer-accuracy lift versus latency/cost delta to confirm the overhead pays; (5) cache sub-answers: frequent sub-questions (e.g. “2022 revenue”) can be cached and reused. In a line: SubQuestion is a premium part for questions that really have several sub-needs — don't leave it on by default.
💭 发散思考（没有标准答案）💭 Open questions (no single right answer)
  • “对比 A、B 两份合同的违约条款差异”为什么适合 sub-question？（提示：拆成两个子问 / 各自检索 / 再对比汇总）Why is “compare the breach-clause differences between contracts A and B” a good fit for sub-question? (Hint: split into two sub-questions / retrieve each / then compare and aggregate)
第七部分 · 超越文本 RAG

31 · 结构化输出

写入路径Write path加载Load切块SplitEmbedEmbed存储Store索引Index
查询路径Query path检索Retrieve后处理Post-process合成Synthesize回答Answer

到这里，RAG 的输出一直是“一段自然语言”——给人读很顺，可一旦要把它接进下游程序（写进数据库、触发工作流、做条件判断），麻烦就来了：你得用正则、字符串切割去“猜”LLM 这次把金额写在哪一行、日期是什么格式。措辞一变、模型一升级，解析脚本就碎。这一课换一种拿结果的方式：别让 LLM 写一段话你再去 parse，直接让它产出一个 Pydantic 对象——字段和类型都是你预先声明的，模型必须照着填，框架还会校验。一句话：类型即契约，LLM 直接交回一个校验过的结构，下游 invoice.total 拿来就用，再没有脆弱的解析这一环。Up to here, RAG's output has always been “a piece of natural language” — nice for a human to read, but the moment you need to feed it into downstream code (write to a database, trigger a workflow, branch on a condition), the trouble starts: you must use regex and string-splitting to “guess” which line the LLM put the amount on and what format the date took. Change the wording or upgrade the model and the parsing script breaks. This lesson swaps the way you collect the result: instead of having the LLM write prose you then parse, have it emit a Pydantic object directly — the fields and types are declared up front by you, the model must fill them in, and the framework validates them. In a line: the type is the contract — the LLM hands back a validated structure, and downstream invoice.total just works, with the fragile parsing step gone entirely.

自由文本 + 手工 parseFree text + manual parse
LLM 写一段话 → 正则/分割提字段 → 措辞一变就碎
LLM writes prose → regex/split fields → breaks when wording shifts
vs
结构化输出Structured output
LLM 直接产出 Pydantic 对象 → 类型校验 → 下游直接用
LLM emits a Pydantic object → type-validated → ready downstream
把“解析自由文本”换成“契约化的类型”swap ‘parse free text’ for ‘a typed contract’

痛点：用正则/手工 parse 自由文本，脆弱易碎The pain: parsing free text with regex/by hand is brittle

朴素做法是让 LLM“用文字描述”结果，再写代码把字段抠出来：正则匹配“总计：¥1,200”、按冒号切“Vendor: Acme”…… demo 里跑得通，但有三个结构性脆点：① 措辞漂移——同一个 prompt，模型今天写“总计”、明天写“合计金额”，正则就漏了；② 格式不稳——日期一会儿“2024-01-05”、一会儿“Jan 5, 2024”，类型转换处处是坑；③ 静默失败——parse 不到时往往返回空串或默认值，错误一路混进下游，等发现时已经写进库。本质问题是：自由文本没有契约，你在用字符串处理去逼近一个本该是结构化的东西——解析脚本永远在追着模型的措辞跑。
The naive approach has the LLM “describe the result in words” and then writes code to dig the fields out: regex-match “Total: ¥1,200”, colon-split “Vendor: Acme”… it runs in a demo, but has three structural weak points: (1) wording drift — with the same prompt the model writes “Total” today and “Amount due” tomorrow, and the regex misses it; (2) unstable formats — a date is “2024-01-05” one time and “Jan 5, 2024” the next, so type conversion is a minefield; (3) silent failure — when a parse misses it often returns an empty string or a default, and the error slips downstream until it has already been written to the store. The root issue: free text has no contract, and you're using string handling to approximate something that should have been structured — the parser is forever chasing the model's phrasing.

Pydantic program：直接让 LLM 产出对象，类型即契约Pydantic program: have the LLM emit an object directly — the type is the contract

结构化输出把顺序倒过来：先用 Pydantic 的 BaseModel 把你要的形状写成一个类——Invoice 有 vendor: str、total: float、due_date: str——这个类就是契约。把它交给一个 program，program 负责把 schema 塞进给 LLM 的指令、解析模型回的内容、再用 Pydantic 校验，最后交还一个真正的 Invoice 对象。于是下游不再 parse 字符串，而是直接 invoice.total + tax：字段一定存在、类型一定正确，是被校验保证过的。LLM 仍然在“生成”，但它生成的目标从“一段话”变成了“一个对象”——你拿到的不再是待解析的文本，而是即用的数据。
Structured output flips the order: first write the shape you want as a Pydantic BaseModel class — Invoice has vendor: str, total: float, due_date: str — and that class is the contract. Hand it to a program, which injects the schema into the LLM's instructions, parses what the model returns, validates it with Pydantic, and hands back an actual Invoice object. Downstream no longer parses strings but writes invoice.total + tax directly: the field is guaranteed to exist and the type to be right, because it was validation-guaranteed. The LLM still “generates”, but the target of generation shifts from “a paragraph” to “an object” — what you get back is no longer text to parse but data ready to use.
声明 Pydantic 模型 → 交给 program → 拿回校验过的对象：下游 invoice.total 直接用，没有正则Declare a Pydantic model → hand it to a program → get back a validated object: downstream invoice.total just works, no regex
from pydantic import BaseModel
from llama_index.core.program import LLMTextCompletionProgram

class Invoice(BaseModel):
    vendor: str
    total: float
    due_date: str

program = LLMTextCompletionProgram.from_defaults(
    output_cls=Invoice,
    prompt_template_str="Extract the invoice fields from:\n{doc}",
)
invoice = program(doc=text)     # -> Invoice(vendor=..., total=..., due_date=...)
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
program/llm_program.py · LLMTextCompletionProgram — 按 Pydantic 模型约束 LLM 输出为结构化对象。constrains LLM output to a structured Pydantic object.

两条路：prompt 模板塞 schema vs 函数调用更稳Two routes: stuff the schema into a prompt vs function calling for more stability

落地有两条路，区别在“怎么逼模型守约”。① LLMTextCompletionProgram（纯 prompt 模板路线）：把 schema 的描述写进提示词，请模型“按这个 JSON 形状回”，再解析它回的文本。胜在不挑模型（任何会生成文本的 LLM 都能用），但约束是“软”的——模型可能多写一句解释、少个引号，解析就得容错、重试。② FunctionCallingProgram（函数调用路线）：把 Pydantic 模型当成一个“函数签名”交给模型原生的 function/tool calling 能力，模型在 API 层就被约束着按字段产出，结构更稳、更少跑偏，代价是要模型支持函数调用。经验法则：模型支持就优先函数调用，更稳；要兼容老模型或本地小模型才退回纯 prompt 模板——而 llm.structured_predict 正是把这条法则做成默认：它自动按模型能力选路（支持函数调用就用，否则回退到 prompt 模板），不用你手动二选一。一个易错点：structured_predict 收的是一个 PromptTemplate，不是裸字符串。
There are two routes in practice, differing in “how you force the model to honor the contract”. (1) LLMTextCompletionProgram (pure prompt-template route): write the schema's description into the prompt, ask the model to “reply in this JSON shape”, then parse the text it returns. Its win is being model-agnostic (any text-generating LLM works), but the constraint is “soft” — the model might add a sentence of explanation or drop a quote, so parsing needs tolerance and retries. (2) FunctionCallingProgram (function-calling route): hand the Pydantic model to the model's native function/tool-calling ability as a “function signature”, so the model is constrained to emit by field at the API level — more stable, less drift — at the cost of needing a model that supports function calling. Rule of thumb: prefer function calling when the model supports it; fall back to the pure prompt template only to support older or small local models — and llm.structured_predict bakes that rule in as the default: it auto-picks the route by model capability (function calling if supported, else falls back to the prompt-template route), so you don't choose by hand. One easy slip: structured_predict takes a PromptTemplate, not a bare string.
对比项AspectLLMTextCompletionProgramLLMTextCompletionProgramFunctionCallingProgramFunctionCallingProgram
约束来自Constraint fromprompt 里塞 schema 描述（软约束）schema stuffed into the prompt (soft)模型原生函数调用（硬约束）the model's native function calling (hard)
稳定性Stability较弱，需容错/重试weaker, needs tolerance/retries更稳，少跑偏steadier, less drift
模型要求Model needs任何会生成文本的 LLMany text-generating LLM需支持 function/tool callingmust support function/tool calling
何时用When兼容老 / 本地小模型for older / small local models模型支持就优先prefer it when supported
🔬 源码对应🔬 In the source
program/function_program.py · FunctionCallingProgram — 把 Pydantic 模型包成工具，用模型的函数调用能力产出结构——和 agent 调工具同源。wraps the Pydantic model as a tool and uses the model's function-calling to emit structure — the same path as agent tool-calling.
一行版：structured_predict 用模型的函数调用直接产出 Invoice——注意第二个参数是 PromptTemplateOne-liner: structured_predict uses the model's function calling to emit Invoice directly — note the 2nd arg is a PromptTemplate
from llama_index.core.prompts import PromptTemplate

invoice = llm.structured_predict(
    Invoice,
    PromptTemplate("Extract from: {doc}"),   # 收 PromptTemplate，不是裸字符串
    doc=text,
)
